bod gangs can gyi grub mtha' ris med kyi mkhas dbang brgya dang brgyad cu lhag gi gsung 'bum so so'i dkar chag phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa shes bya'i gter mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
bar cha mi rigs dpe mdzod khang gis bsgrigs pa /
mi rigs dpe skrun khang /
gleng gzhi /
bod rigs ni rang rgyal gyi lo rgyus yun ring ldan pa'i mi rigs rlabs chen zhig yin la /
las la brtson zhing dpa' ba dang /
blo rig ldan pa zhig kyang red /
rlabs chen gyi mes rgyal gsar gtod byed pa'i go rim nang du byas rjes 'od stong 'bar ba bzhag yod cing /
lo rgyus 'phel rgyas kyi chu klung ring po 'di'i nang du bod kyi mi rigs dang mi rigs gzhan dag thun mong thog nas mes rgyal gyi rig gzhung 'od stong rab tu 'phro ba zhig gsar gtod byas yod pa red /
bod yig gi dpe rnying 'di dag ni mes rgyal mi rigs kyi rig gzhung gi nor mdzod nang gi mu tig gzi 'od rab tu 'phro ba zhig red /
bod yig gi dpe rnying de dag dus rabs bcu gcig pa'i gong la sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab bsgyur rgyu de gtso bor byas shing /
de ni bod kyi btsan po mes dbon rnam gsum gyi dus nas 'go tshugs pa zhig red /
btsan po khri srong lde btsan gyi skabs su bsgyur zin pa'i gsung rab thams cad dkar chag tu bkod pa 'phang thang ma dang /
mchims phu ma /
ldan dkar ma gsum yod rung 'phang mchims gnyis kyi dkar chag 'thor gyar du song bas ldan dkar ma tsam las ma lus pa de ni bstan 'gyur gyi sna tshogs zhes pa'i khrod du bzhugs pa 'di yin /
dkar chag 'di'i nang bka' bstan gnyis sde tshan bcu dgur phyes te theg chen dang /
theg dman /
mdo phyogs /
sngags phyogs /
sde snod gsum bcas kyi go rim ltar phye thog mdo sde'i sde snod nang phar phyin dang /
phal chen /
dkon brtsegs /
bsdus pa chen po bcas kyi go rim ltar bsgrigs 'dug de ni gsung rab sde tshan dbye ba'i srol thog mar gtod pa zhig red /
bod la sangs rgyas chos lugs dar ba dang chabs cig chos lugs grub mtha' 'dra min 'ga' re byung ba'i 'go tshugs shing /
dus rabs bcu gcig pa tshun tsam la gsung rab de dag gi dgongs 'grel dang /
lo rgyus /
skad yig rig gnas skor sogs kyi rtsom  rigs je mang du phyin te rtsom rigs kyi glegs bam ha cang mang po zhig dar ba red /
de dag ni bod yig gi dpe rnying nang gi grub cha gal chen zhig red /
nang don mdor bsdus na rig gnas che ba lnga ste bzo rig pa dang /
gso ba rig pa /
sgra rig pa /

rgyal rabs /
mi rigs bar gyi 'brel ba'i skor gyi lo rgyus /
chos 'byung /

gdung rabs /
rang rnam /
gsang ba'i rnam thar sogs dang /
gnas yig dang /

gzhan yang mgur ma dang /
legs bshad /

gna' dus rgya gar gyi skad yig saM skr-i ta'i sgra rig pa dang /
gtan tshigs rig pa /
snyan ngag sogs gsal bshad byed pa'i mchan 'grel skor gyi rtsom rigs kyang mi nyung ba zhig yod pa red /
de dag khyon yongs kyi grangs 'bor ji tsam yod pa ni re re bzhin brjod kyis mi lang ngo / /
gong gsal rig gnas shul bzhag 'di dag ni bod kyi sangs rgyas chos lugs dang bod rigs kyi rig gzhung la brtag dpyad byed rgyur blangs na rdzogs rgyu med pa dang spyad na 'dzad mtha' med pa'i bang mdzod cig yin pas rang cag gis brtsi mthong chen po byed 'os pa zhig red /
gsung 'bum skor gyi rtsom rigs ni bka' bstan 'gyur gyi khongs su ma gtogs pa'i dpe rnying rtsom rigs kyi grub cha gtso bo zhig yin la bod yig dpe rnying gi bcud lta bu red /
dus rabs bco brgyad pa'i mjug la klong rdol bla ma ngag dbang blo bzang gis <<bka' gdams pa dang dge lugs pa'i bla ma rags rim gyi gsung 'bum mtshan tho>> bsgrigs pa de'i nang la gsung 'bum khag bzhi bcu tsam las /
bu ston rin chen grub dang /
rje tsong kha pa sogs mkhas dbang kha shas kyi gsung 'bum le tshan dpe tho zhib phra tsam dang /
de min mdor bsdus shig bkod 'dug cing /
dus rabs bcu dgu pa'i dkyil la drung chen shes rab rgya mtshos <<dpe rgyun dkon pa 'ga' zhig gi tho yig don gnyer yid kyi  kun dA bzhad pa'i zla 'od 'bum gyi snye ma>> zhes pa bsgrigs pa de'i nang sde tshan bcu gnyis su phyes te gsung 'bum khag dgu bcu'i mtshan tho bkod 'dug lor bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du snum par thog dkod pa'i <<bla brang dgon pa'i dpe cha spyi'i dkar chag>> nang la sde khag che ba bcu bdun bgos shing /
gsung 'bum skor la mkhas dbang yi dpe tho bkod 'dug bod rigs kyi rig gnas bya gzhag shul 'dzin dang dar spel byed rgyu dang /
mi rigs khag gi rig gnas brje res byed rgyu /
thun mong du dar rgyas phun sum tshogs pa yong bar skul spel gtong rgyu /
mi rigs kyi tshan rig zhib 'jug gi bya ba byed rgyu /
dngos po dang bsam blo'i dpal yon gnyis kyi 'dzugs skrun byed rgyu bcas la zhabs 'degs zhu ba'i ched du 'di ga dpe mdzod khang gi bod yig dpe rnying legs sgrig byed pa'i rmang gzhi'i thog 'di gar bzhugs yod pa'i bod yig dpe rnying nang gsung 'bum skor gyi dkar chag zhib phra bsgrigs nas /
thog mar deb 'di bsgrigs pa yin /
deb 'di'i nang khyon bsdoms mkhas dbang brgya dang brgyad cu tsam gyi gsung 'bum 'dus yod cing /
deb gsum du bgos te rim pas par bskrun byed rgyu yin /
gsung 'bum skor gyi dkar chag 'di ni dpe cha dang dpyad gzhi sogs 'tshol bde ched bod rgya skad gnyis shan sbyar byas nas bkod yod pa'i lag cha lta bu'i deb cig yin /
'on kyang 'di ga'i dpe mdzod khang du yod pa'i dpe cha'i gnas tshul mtshon pa tsam zhig las /
bod yig dpe rnying nang gsung 'bum skor gyi rtsom rig yod do cog gi rnam pa yongs su mtshon mi thub /
bod yig dpe rnying rnams la dpe ming rgyas pa dang bsdus pa gnyis yod cing /
dpe ming rgyas pa de dag ha cang ring bas blor nges dka' ba dang /
lhag par du thun mong ma yin pa'i khyad chos dmigs bsal re yod la /
tha snyad dang mngon brjod rnam grangs mang bas klog pa pos go dka' ba zhig dang /
dpe ming kha byang bsdus pa de dag ni ming 'dra ba mang bas dkar chag bzo dus rnyog 'dzing yong sla ba zhig red /
der brten dpe cha'i kha byang yongs rdzogs ji bzhin bshus nas dkar chag bzos yod /

mi shugs mi 'dang ba /

khong ni yab tshe mgon rgyal dang yum hal can khu'am bod ming blo bzang nyi ma gnyis la sras bzhi dang sras mo bzhi ste ming sring brgyad yod pa'i nang gi che shos yin /

dgung lo bdun par phebs pa na /
a khu dge tshul zhig yod pa de'i mdun thog mar sog yig dang de nas bod yig gzab gshar sogs sbyangs /
lo der chas pa blo bzang 'phrin las kyi drung nas rab tu byung zhing dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa zhus /
ming blo bzang tshul khrims zhes pa btags /
gzhan phan byang chub gling gi dgon par tshogs su zhugs /
lo mang ring a khu dge rgan du bsten nas shes bya mtha' dag 'bad pas sbyangs /
dgung lo bco lnga pa shing khyi lor /

a khu dang gcung gcig sras mo gsum mnyam du grongs /

de nas mi ring bar /
a chi thu no mon han blo bzang bstan 'dzin drung nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes /

de nas tshur phebs /

zab chos mang po zhus /
dgung lo nyer gsum pa chu pho rta'i lor zla ba brgyad par pe cing yung he gung du slob gnyer la phebs /

a kyA blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan khong gi bla ma gtso bor gyur /
khong ni yon tan kho na do gnyer mdzad pa las /

khrom gyi tshong 'dus su lan gnyis ma gtogs byon ma myong /
skabs der lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje /

pag shi bla ma ngag dbang dpal ldan /

a kyA'i gsung 'bum pod gnyis po legs bsgrigs dang shing par gyi ma yig 'bri ba dang par zhu sogs tshang ma khong gis mdzad /

tshang mas dge bshes dge bshes zhes bos pas /
cha har dge bshes zhes pa'i mtshan rgyun 'jags su gyur /

od nyid gu shrI rin po che'i drung du sngags phyogs kyi chos skor gsan /

de nas sku mtshams lo gnyis bzhugs te /

dgongs rdzogs legs par bsgrubs /
de nas dgung lo so drug pa lug lo'i ston kha nas sa pho khyi lo'i bar lo bzhi tsam dpe mtshams bzhugs /

dgung lo zhe gcig pa lcags pho byi ba'i lor /

shing par gyi ma yig khong gis phyag bris mdzad /
glang gi lor rang yul du log nas /
paN chen gyi gsang rnam gsang ba'i lung zhes pa de sog skad du bsgyur /

'brug lor dkar po ri'i dgon pa dga' ldan chos 'dzin gling gsar du btab pa'i grabs bkod mdzad /
me mo lug gi lor 'du khang chen mo bzhengs grub /
de nas mu mthud de lha khang dang rten gsar bzhengs mdzad /
dge 'dun pa'i bca' yig sogs kyang gsar du brtsams /
lug lo'i ston khar lnga pa'i gsung lugs zung gi  bslab bya mu thi la'i phreng ba sog skad du bsgyur /

... byang phyogs po red ljongs kyi bstan pa'i mnga' bdag sems dpa' chen po mkhan chen paN+Di ta d+harma rA dza skal bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam par thar pa skal ldan rna ba'i bcud len snyan pa'i tshangs dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

mdo smad sa'i thig ler /
khywa dge'i yul gyi bye brag se tshang zhes pa'i yul grur /
zu ru 'phrin las tshang gi khyim du /
yab be ri grub che'i tsha bo bstan pa dang /
yum lha mo mtsho gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i sa mo phag gi lor zla ba dgu pa la sku bltams /
byis pa'i dus su lha bab cig gis 'jigs med bstan 'dzin zhes pa'i mtshan gsol /
dgung lo bzhi lnga tsam la 'jam bzhad gsum pa thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtshos /
rgya mkhar ba dkon mchog bstan pa'i nyi ma'i yang srid du ngos 'dzin mdzad /
dgung lo bdun par /
bla ma gong ma'i gdan sa dga' ldan bshad sgrub dar rgyas gling du phebs te gdan khrir bzhugs /
sa dmar chos 'dzin klog gi slob dpon du bsten nas sbyor klog 'don chog rnams rdzogs par sbyangs /
mkhan po dkon mchog bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan spyan sngar rab byung dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
dkon mchog lung rigs rgya mtsho zhes pa'i mtshan gnang /
dgung lo bcu gcig par bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du phebs nas thos bsam gling du grwa sar zhugs /
'jam bzhad sku thog gsum pa'i gser zhal thog mar mjal /
dpal mang mkhas chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan mdun nas skyabs 'gro'i khrid gsan /
rdo rams pa rda rig blo bzang dge rgan du bsten nas /
tshad ma'i skor bsdus grwa sogs legs par sbyangs /
skabs de dag tu sde khri rin po che 'jam dbyangs thub bstan nyi ma dang /
dpal mang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan sogs la dbang lung mang po zhus shing /
khyad par rje btsun shes rab rgya mtsho'i spyan sngar rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che yongs rdzogs kyi ljags lung zhus /

dpe brjod kyang rdzogs par phul bas /

sa ris /

ming ngag dbang dge 'dun sangs rgyas rgya mtsho zhes pa gnang /
bde mchog dang /
gdugs dkar /
'jigs byed sogs kyi dbang dang /
rgyan 'jug gnyis kyi lung sogs dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi ngoms med myong /
de nas mi ring bar sog yul du maN+Dal su me dgon dang /
hal har sogs su zhabs kyis gcags /
ser skya stong phrag mang por dam pa'i chos kyi gru char 'bebs /
de nas so nyi g.yon ru'i yul grur brgyud de /
rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar gnas mjal du phebs /
tshur log zhor pe cing du phebs te tsan+dan jo bo byin rlabs can mjal zhing /
mkhar phyi nang gi tshong 'dus la ltad mor gzigs pa bcas nyin zhag mang tsam 'gor /
de nas rang yul phebs pa'i phyi lor /
rgya bod bar yul 'khrugs rgya chen bslangs nas /
dgon sde 'ga' yang  'byung ba me la bsregs /
shin tu gces pa'i mi mang po rin chen srog dang bral /
mtha' dbus kun tu dmag 'khrug gi me lce mched /
lo 'gar sdug bsngal dang mu ge'i 'jigs pas mnar /
skabs der ngan slong la sbyin pa dang /
dkon mchog la mchod pa sogs thar pa'i sa bon legs par bskrun /
dka' rams 'dzin grwar slebs pa'i phyi lor brda sprod smra ba dngul ra snyan grags mdun du dbyangs can sgra mdo'i ri mo yongs rdzogs /
gtsos kyi a bstan mdun sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas /
rje btsun shes rab rgya mtsho'i spyan sngar /
snyan ngag rtsa 'grel /
sgra mdo dbyangs 'char gyi 'grel pa mchog dga' sogs kyi lung bcas thun mong gi rig pa'i gnas kun la sbyangs pa nan smin mdzad /
brag dgon pa bstan pa rab rgyas drung nas kyang chos bka' ci rigs gsan /
dgung grangs sum cur phebs pa rab byung bco lnga pa'i sa pho 'brug gi lo la dbus lha ldan du chas /
chab mdo nas brgyud de lha sar 'byor /
jo bo rin po che sogs rten khyad 'phags rnams mjal skor rjes 'bras spungs su bkra shis sgo mang grwa tshang du lo gcig tsam chos grwar 'grim /
de nas dpal bsam yas gtsug lag khang /
khra 'brug lho brag phyogs kyi mar mi'i gdan sa /
'brong rtse'i zhwa lu'i gser khang /

sa skya dang snar thang sogs gnas chen rnams mjal zhing /

shar rtse /
dkyil khang bcas grwa tshang gsum gyi mkhas mang dbus su /
nyin gsum gyi bar tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi dam bca' bzhag paN chen rin po che thugs dgyes pa chen pos bka' mol yun ring gnang zhing /
byin rten dang stod 'gag ther sham sogs dngos po'i gsol ras gya nom pa bstsal /
de nas dbus gtsang dgon gnas rnams su zla re'am zhag grangs 'ga' re tsam la sgrub pa nyams len mdzad cing /
tshe gcig ring dbus lha ldan gyi zhing khams su sgrub pa snying por mdzad de bzhugs snyam yang /
rang yul du phebs dgos kyi 'phrin yig yang nas yang du 'byor bar brten /
byang lam brgyud nas rang yul du log skabs der khong gi dgon pa ni rgyud pa grwa tshang tsam lus pa ma gtogs /
grwa shag rnams kyang zhig ral du gyur /
chos sde'i gling bar yang rtswa dang ldum bus gang /
grwa btsun rnams kyang grong chog kho nar rgyug dgon par ser mo ba sdod mkhan med cing khyi ldom rnams kyi rtse gnas su gyur nas nyams rgud tshad med byung bar brten /
da ni thabs gang zhig gis chos sde 'dir nyams gso dang 'phel rgyas su gtong snyam pa'i dgongs pa yang yang 'char /

nyin der kha char 'dres ma babs shing /
rgyab ri'i rtse nas 'brug skad ldir ba sogs rten 'brel legs par 'grig /
de nas rim gyis 'chad nyan dang tshad ma sbyong mkhan gyi grwa btsun lo re bzhin je mang du phyin /
dgon pa'ang yar rgyas su song zhing dge 'dun 'dus sde yang dbyar gyi chu bo ltar gong du 'phel bar gyur /
rjes nas bshad grwa de'i ming thos bsam gling btags /
de nas yang ri bo rtse lngar thengs gnyis pa byon /
zla shas 'gor rjes hor yul so nyi g.yon ru'i gzhis sgar thog  tu phebs /
mkhan po gong ma'i sprul sku dang khong gnyis mnyam du bzhugs /
su me dgon pa dang yon bdag rnams kyi re ba ltar dbang bskur chos bshad mang po mdzad /
skabs der sprul sku dang khong gnyis bar 'khor g.yog ngan pa 'gas phra ma bcug cing /
sprul sku'ang ngan pa'i rjes su phyogs /
khong der bzhugs stabs ma bde nas /
sog hal ha'i phyogs su byon /

sog dgon phal che bar phebs /
khyad par u ru sog dang 'dabs 'brel ba'i yul gyi ham nyag dgon du'ang phebs nas /
pir tse grwa tshang la gdugs dkar lha mang gi dbang sogs bskur /
dngul srang 'khor sum brgya lhag btang nas /

de nas mi ring bar rang yul du tshur phebs ma thag bkra shis 'khyil gyi dus 'khor grwa tshang gi khrir bzhugs /
'chad nyan dang gtong sgo mang 'gyed sogs dge 'dun mnyes pa'i bya ba'ang 'bad pas bsgrubs par brten snyan grags chen por gyur /
dgung grangs lnga bcu nga gcig pa rab byung bco lnga pa'i sa mo glang gi lo'i dbyar khar bla brang bkra shis 'khyil gyi tshogs chen khrir bzhugs /
dgung lo nga bdun par bde mo thang dga' ldan chos 'khor gling gi tshogs chen khrir bzhugs /
hal ha'i sbyin bdag rnams nas der phebs dgos pa'i zhu mchid dang gdan 'dren gyi pho nya yang yang 'byor bas hor gyi yul du lan bzhi pa phebs /
dgung grangs re gcig pa sa mo phag lo'i ston mjug tu rang yul du chibs kha bsgyur /
phyi lo'i smon lam chen mor bkra shis 'khyil du phebs nas dgon par rten bzhag dang /
grwa mang la 'gyed sogs rgya chen phul /

... ka bskal bzang sangs rgyas stong phrag gi phyag mchod smon lam dang bcas pa bsod nams kyi myu gu 'phel bar byed pa'i bdud rtsi'i char chen zhes bya ba bzhugs / /

... 'phags pa thar pa chen po phyogs su rgyas pa'i mdo sde 'don pa'i cho ga sdig sgrib thams cad rab tu 'khru bar byed pa'i bdud rtsi'i char chen zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bla ma dang 'jam dbyangs zung 'brel gyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs myur 'jug ces bya ba bzhugs / /
... theg pa chen po'i gso sbyong gi sdom pa len pa'i cho ga thar pa'i bde lam zhes bya ba bzhugs / /

... bsnyen gnas bsrungs pa'i phan yon mdor bsdus pa dad pa'i myu gu zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... bla ma dang gsang ba 'dus pa dbyer med kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor dge legs kun stsol zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

chos 'chad nyan dang sgrigs lam /
cho ga phyag len sogs la dag ther dang do dam nan smin mdzad /
long skabs gang yod du mdo sngags kyi gzhung la gzigs zhib dang /
rig pa'i gnas gzhan dag la'ang thugs sbyong yang yang mdzad /
dgung lo sum cu pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i me byi lo'i zla ba gsum pa'i tshes gsum la sku 'bum byams pa gling gi gdan khrir phebs /
dus 'khor grwa tshang gsar 'dzugs dang /
'du khang gsar bzhengs mdzad /
sa yos lo'i bar lo bzhi'i ring gdan khrir bzhugs /
sa yos lor stag 'tsher blo bzang mkhas grub nyi mas khri chen du bskos /
dgung lo so lnga pa lcags sbrul lo'i zla ba drug pa'i tshes bcu gsum la sgar btegs te sog po'i yul grur brgyud zla ba bcu gcig pa'i mjug la pe cing du 'byor /
sku zhabs a rgya tshang gi bla brang du bzhugs /
tsan dan jo bo sogs rten khyad 'phags rnams 'jal skor dang /
gong ma rabs so so'i pho brang dang /
skyed tshal rnams su gzigs mor phebs /
chu pho rta'i gnam lo gsar du bzhad pa'i dus ston skabs su /
lcang skya rin po cher lo gsar phyag 'bul zhus shing thugs snang gshin pa'i gsung gleng mdzad /
gong ma'i skyed tshal yu hwa yon du lcang skya'i zhabs zhu pa byas nas gzigs mor phebs /
pe cing zla ba gnyis tsam 'gor /
chu rta lor zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu dgu la pe cing nas btegs te sog  yul du phebs /
sog ho sho'i dgon sde rnams su dbang bskur chos bshad dang /
dge bsnyen dang rab byung gi sdom pa 'bogs pa sogs dam pa chos kyi phyag las lo brgyad tsam mdzad /
dgung lo zhe gsum pa sa mo glang gi lo'i zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes nyi shu la sog yul nas chas te /
lcags stag lo'i zla ba dang por sku 'bum du 'byor /
me bya lor bka' 'gyur ba dkon mchog dpal sku 'bum du gdan drangs nas rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro cog gi lung zhus /
dgung lo re gnyis pa sa sprel lo'i zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bcu gcig la chu bzang rin po ches nan zhus mdzad par brten bya khyung dgon pa'i khri chen la bzhugs /
khri ston gzabs rgyas byas shing /
zla ba drug pa'i tshes bco lnga la dbyar gnas gsar du btsugs /
dgung lo re bzhi pa lcags khyi lo'i zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes bcu gsum la khri pa dgongs pa zhus te /
mkhan po bskal bzang nor bu khri par bskos /
zla ba lnga pa'i tshes gcig la bya khyung nas btegs /
zla ba lnga pa'i tshes gsum la sku 'bum du byon /
zla ba brgyad par 'jam bzhad blo bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtsho sku 'bum du phebs pa mjal zhing /
mi ring bar bkra shis 'khyil du log phebs pa /
khong bkra shis thang gi bar chibs skyel du byon /
sa rta lo'i zla ba lnga par thu'u bkwan chos kyi nyi ma'i sprul sku nas /
khong dgon lung du gdan drangs nas dbang lung sogs chos bka' mang po zhus /
dgung lo don gnyis su phebs pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i sa pho rta lo'i zla ba dgu par a b+ha ka wang gis nan gyis gdan zhus byas par brten sog yul du lan rting mar zhabs kyis bcags /
snga phyir sog po'i yul du lan bdun byon /
de ga'i dgon sde che phra yongs la zhabs kyis bcags /
bla dpon mang por dbang lung bshad khrid sogs chos kyi sbyin pa rgya che bstsal /
lo so lnga'i ring sog yul du dam chos spel zhing sku tshe tha ma'i cha de'ang sog po'i dad ldan rnams la phul /
dgung lo don bzhi pa lcags pho sprel lo'i zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bzhi la ho ching wang gis khong pe li'i dgon nas murge phyogs su gdan drangs /
murge dgon su mu smon 'phel gling gi dge 'dun pa rnams kyis phebs bsu rgya chen mdzad /
'du khang du byon nas kun la phyag dbang dang zhal mjal mdzad /
nyin gnyis pa nas dus 'khor dbang chen bskur ba'i sta gon byas /
'on kyang dbang yang sta gon tsam la lus te zla de'i tshes brgyad pa'i nyin gung gi dus su dgongs pa rdzogs so / /

dpyid chos la slob gnyer gyi mgo btsugs /

sku chung ngu'i dus nas mkhyen rab kyi rtsal rdzogs pas 'bri klog sogs tshegs med du mkhyen /

e waM thar pa rtse'i mkhan chen byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med kyi yang srid du ngos bzung /

bde dgyes gsang gsum /

gangs can gyi ljongs su man ngag sngon gyi phyag srol ma nyams par yod pa thams cad so so'i khungs dang 'brel ba'i yongs 'dzin gtsug tu bsten te smin byed kyi dbang dang /

rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che dang /
rnying ma rgyud 'bum /
bstan 'gyur gyi khrod las lung rgyun gang bzhugs so cog gi gtsos 'phags bod ris med kyi gsung chos yongs bsdoms glegs bam bdun brgya tsam gyi bklag lung rnams sku ngal khyad du bsad de 'bad brtson chen pos gsan bzhes mdzad cing /
sgom sgrub nyams len mdzad pas nyams rtogs khyad par can thugs la 'khrungs /

skye 'gro rnams smin cing grol ba'i lam la bkod /

sa skya'i khri chen bkra shis rin chen /

si tu sku phreng bcu pa dang bcu gcig pa /

dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas /
brag g.yab no min han chen po /
li thang mkhan chen byams pa phun tshogs /
hor khang pa rgyal ba sogs ri bo dge ldan pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po dag dang /
g.yung drung bon gyi bstan pa 'dzin pa sogs bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu grangs las 'das pa byon /
dad ldan slob tshogs kyis phul ba'i zang zing gi dngos po gang byung thams cad kyis sku rten gser zangs las bzhengs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi snang brnyan nyis stong tsam dang /
gsung rten shing par du bkod pa po ti bzhi bcu la nye ba dang /
bris ma sogs po ti nyis stong tsam dang /
thugs rten lhun grub steng gi mchod sdong chen mo gtsos brgya lhag tsam gser zangs kyis bskrun /

rgya bod kyi mi dpon /

rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i sa pho sprel lo la 'khrungs /
dgung lo drug par chos rje don grub rgya mtsho'i mdun nas rab tu byung /

de nas sog yul du phebs /

me pho rta lo la gtsang phyogs su phyag phebs /
snar thang /
byang chen /
rta nag ri khud rnams la byon te lo lnga drug ring 'chad nyan 'phel bar mdzad /
lcags pho phyi lo la snar thang du 'jug pa'i rnam bshad dgogs pa rab tu gsal ba'i me long gi rtsoms yang mdzad /
chu pho byi ba'i lo la tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi TI ka rtsom par mdzad /
sa skya dang snar thang du phebs te rtsa she'i rnam bshad rin po che'i phreng ba yang brtsams shing 'chad nyan gyi sgo nas gtan la phab /
dge sbyong dkar po bas rta nag tu spyan drangs te ri khud chos sde phul /
der lo shas bzhugs /
sngar tsong kha pa chen po la tshad ma rnam nges kyi dogs gcod gsan pa'i zin bris dang /
rgyal tshab rje la rnam 'grel gsan pa'i gsung rgyun rnams la gzhir byas te tshad ma'i bstan bcos chen po rig pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba me sbrul lor rdzogs par grub /
sngar mkhas grub rje la chos 'brel tsam las ma byung /
da dus 'khor gyi chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa zhig zhu bar da lan 'gro snyam du dgongs te gsang thabs mdzad nas byon /
ri bo dge 'phel du phebs /
de'i tshe dge ldan du mkhas grub rje sku mya ngan las 'das zer ba'i skad cha gsan nas da re zhig phyin kyang don ma grub snyam nas der zla gcig tsam sku mtshams mdzad de bzhugs /
sa pho rta lo la dge 'phel nas dbus phyogs su snye mo rgyal byed tshal brgyud dga' ldan du phebs /
byang rtse pa chos rje nam mkha' dpal ba'i drung nas dbang lung man ngag sogs mang po zhus /
kong po lnga ri dang /
mdo smad sogs su sgrub pa la 'byon pa'i thugs rtse gtad yod na'ang de dus gtsang phyogs nas gdan 'dren pa slebs te gtsang phyogs su mdo sngags kyi bshad nyan mdzad na bsam grub rtse pa sogs kyis sbyin bdag mdzad pa yod pas cis kyang 'byon dgos zhes nan gyis zhus par brten lcags pho sprel lo la slar yang gtsang phyogs su phebs /
snar thang du 'dul ba'i gleng 'bum chen mo dang so thar gyi TI ka brtsams /
de dus dgongs par snga dus bod 'dir lo paN rnams kyi ring la bshad nyan dar bar byung 'dug kyang gzhi gsum gyi phyag lan cher ma byung /
da 'dul ba'i bslab khrims rnam par dag pa gzhir bzung ste de'i steng nas bshad nyan gtso bor byed pa zhig bya dgos dgongs te /
de'i rten 'brel du bslab khrims kyi bca' yig chen mo zhig chu pho 'brug lo la dpal byang chub chen por ljags rtsom mdzad /
de nas bzung ste gzhi gsum gyi phyag len bar ma chad par yod pa yin /
de nas snar thang du rje 'di pas nye gnas chen po don grub grags pa la !!ngas chos phyogs nas 'chad nyan byas te lag rjes shig 'jog pa dang 'jig rten zang zing gi longs spyod kyis rten bzhengs zhig byas te lag rjes dod pa zhig byas na bsam pas rten de bzhugs sa zhig snar thang gi spyi sgos gang rung zhig tu dkar me'i rgyun gang 'byor zhig dang bcas te byung na bsam pa yin pas 'dod mos ltar cis kyang dgos'' zhes zhus par don ma thob /
seng ge rtser zhus nas dpal sdings sam gangs can gang rung zhig dgos zhes zhus pa'ang dgon khag gzhan gyis chags sdang gis bkag ste ma byung /
don de ji ltar byas nas 'ong snyam du dgongs pa btang bas sngar rje shes rab seng ge bsam grub rtse nas snar thang la byon rim bzhin bkra shis lhun po'i dgon sa 'di la phyag mdzub gtad de sa phyogs 'di na dge 'dun grub mgo bo skya yer yer chos 'chad kyin yod pa zhig rgyun du 'char snang 'ongs kyi 'dug gsungs pa zhig yang yang yod par brten sa phyogs de ga rang du bzang bar gzigs te dgon pa 'debs pa'i thugs thag bcad /
bsam grub rtse'i brag dmar bla brang du rten bzhengs kyi 'go btsugs /
thog ma'i lugs phud du rje btsun sgrol ma'i sku zhig dang /
ston pa'i sku mtho nyer lnga can lugs ma gzi 'od 'bar ba gzungs bzhugs khyad par can gyis bsgrubs pa zhig bzhengs /
sbyin bdag dar rgyas dpon bsod nams dpal bzang gis mdzad nas me mo yos lo'i smin drug zla ba'i yar tshes bzang pos rje rang nyid kyis gtsos sbyin bdag dang bcas pa 'dir phebs te gtsug lag khang dang /
bla brang /
brang khang bcas pa'i 'gram bting ste bkra shis lhun po dpal gyi sde chen po phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba'i gling de btab /
de nas lung nag rdzong dang /
dpal sdings /
snar thang sogs la rim bzhin byon /
'chad nyan rgyun ma chad par mdzad /
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po bzhengs te nang rten ngo mtshar can de la rab gnas dang mnga' gsol rgyas par mdzad /
de nas rnam sras gling du dbyar gnas mdzad pa'i zhabs tog bsam grub rtse nas bsgrubs /
dgag dbye thog nas rje dpon slob rnams bkra shis lhun por phebs te der gzhi phab ste bzhugs pa'i thog ma de nas mdzad /
me sbrul lo'i dgun chos nas 'go brtsams te grwa pa rnams kyis kyang bkra shis lhun por bzhugs pa'i mthil mdzad /
sa pho rta lor rje bla ma 'di ri bo dge ldan gyi mkhan por gdan 'dren pa byung yang /
bkra shis lhun po'i dgon pa 'di btab ma thag tu sog bas rgyun brtan pa zhig ma byung kha dang /
rje btsun tsong kha pa chen po'i bstan pa 'bab zhig la dgongs te 'di gar sdod pa yin gsungs te mi byon par thag bcad /
sa skya pa chos rje seng rgyal gyi drung nas dmar po skor gsum gyi man ngag dang /
rta mgrin yang gsang sogs kyi rjes gnang man ngag rnams zhus /
rje btsun sgrol ma'i gser sku mda' tshad ma sogs sku mang po bzhengs /
de nas shing pho spre'u'i lo la phyogs kyi yig mkhan mang po bsdus te thugs dam bka' 'gyur gyi gsung rab dang gos sku  chen mo dkyus su 'dom bco brgyad dang /
zheng du 'dom bcu gnyis yod pa mtshar zhing byin rlabs dang ldan pa zhig bzhengs te gos sku 'di'i thugs ka na rje rang nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam gyi tshig mang po zhig bris par mdzad /
de nas sku gsung thugs rten gyi rten khyad par can mang po bzhengs pa 'di rnams la rje rang nyid kyis rab gnas kyang mdzad /

ri bo che /
dge ldan /

khro phu /
gnas rnying /
bo dong sogs kyi dgon sde khag la mchod rdzas grangs med par phul zhing /
chu mo sbrul lo'i dgun chos gnyis la grwa pa chig stong drug brgya tsam la gsol phogs dang /
gsol thug sogs kyi zhabs tog legs par bsgrubs te chos 'khor rgya chen po bskor /
shing pho rta lo'i cho 'phrul chen po'i zla ba la gnas rnying rin po ches thog drangs phyogs kyi bu slob kyi bstan 'dzin chen po rnams kyang spyan drangs nas tshogs pa chig stong drug brgya tsam gyi smon lam btsugs /
rje 'di'i sku tshe 'di la 'dul ba'i bslab khrims rnam par dag pa gzhir bzung /
gzhi gsum gyi phyag len ma nyams pa'i ngang nas bshad nyan /
rten bzhengs /

dkon cog gi mchod pa /

shing pho rta lor ston myang stod chab tshan du phebs te /
phu mda'i skye bo'i tshogs mtha' yas pa dag dang /
chos sde che chung na bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun rnams la chos dang byin rlabs kyi bsnyen bkur sogs bdag gir mdzad de snar thang brgyud slar yang bkra shis lhun por phebs /
lo 'di'i zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bdun tsam la /
zhal skyug cung zad 'ong ba'i sku khams ma bde ba tsam yod la /
snyun zug chen po med par cung zad thugs nyob pa'i rnam pa bstan nas sems dpa' chen pos thog drangs slob dpon gzhis bzhugs rnams drung du bos par mdzad /
rje'i zhal nas /
khyed rnams kyis spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang /
sems can gyi bde skyid /
khyad par bkra shis lhun po'i bstan pa la bsams nas ji srid bar du 'dir bzhugs nas bshad sgrub tshul bzhin mdzad na nged kyi bsam pa yang de gas 'grub pa yin zhes zab dang rgya che'i chos bka' mang po bstsal nas de'i mtshan mo thugs dam la rtse gcig tu mnyam par bzhugs te rab byung brgyad pa'i shing rta lo la zhi bar gshegs so / /
gsung rab ni dam chos 'dul ba'i gleng 'bum chen mo /

... tA la'i sku phreng gnyis pa rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho ni gtsang rta nag tu yab kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang /
yum kun dga' bzang mo gnyis kyi sras su rab byung brgyad pa'i me spre lor sku bltams /
dgung lo bcu gcig tu phebs skabs bkra shis lhun po'i gdan sar khri 'don thog mdzad sgo legs par bskyangs /
me rta lor paN chen lung rigs rgya mtsho'i mdun nas dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa bzhes /
mtshan dge 'dun rgya mtsho zhes gsol /
lo de rang gi dgun chos skabs gnas rnying kun dga' bde legs pas mkhan po dang /
paN chen lung rigs rgya mtshos slob dpon mdzad de dge tshul gyi bslab pa bzhes shing /
gnas rnying pa'i lugs kyi mgon po 'khor brgyad kyi rjes gnang sogs chos bka' 'ga' zhig gsan /
tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi gzhung gsan sbyong mdzad /
de rjes paN chen ye shes rtse mo bkra shis lhun po'i gdan sar phebs pa yongs 'dzin du bsten nas mdo sngags kyi dbang lung mang po gsan /
dgung lo bcu drug tsam la snyan ngag gi gzhung la slob gnyer legs par mdzad de blo gros kyi snang ba thogs pa med par rgyas nas rje tsong kha pa sogs la snyan ngag gi tshig rgyan la brten nas bstod pa zhig brtsams pa'i dbu tshugs /
de nas rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sde sogs la phebs /
de skabs snar thang gi mkhan po rgyal ba grags pas dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i yab la ha cang mi mnyes pa'i dbang gis !!mi ? 'di'i bu la thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku skye mi yong '+'+zer ? ba sogs kyis bkra shis lhun por bzhugs bzod mi bde ba'i gnas tshul byung yod kyang /
bzod pa'i go cha snying por 'dzin te bzhugs bzhin pa'i skabs 'bras spungs pa'i gdan rabs brgyad pa 'jam dbyangs legs pa chos 'byor sogs kyis dbus phyogs su spyan drangs /
dgung lo bcu dgu bzhes skabs bkra shis lhun po nas dbus su btegs te dpal ldan 'bras spungs su phebs /
lo gsum ring 'jam dbyangs legs chos kyi drung nas phar tshad dang /
'dul mdzod /
mngon pa gong 'og mdo sde rgyan sogs nang don rig pa'i gzhung lugs du ma'i mdzub khrid dang /
rje yab sras kyi bka' 'bum sogs dbang lung mang po zhig legs par gsan /
dgung lo nyi shu'i thog gnas rnying kun dga' bde legs kyis mkhan po dang /
'jam dbyangs legs chos kyis las slob mdzad de bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes /
byang ra sgreng du byon nas rten rnams mjal /
de nas lho kha bsam yas dang /
'phyongs rgyas /
rtsed thang sogs la zhabs kyis bcags te dam pa'i chos kyi sbyin pa tshad med bstsal /
dgung lo nyer lngar phebs dus nang so brag dkar ba srid chos rgyal  pos mthun rkyen sbyar te brag yer par drang nges rnam 'byed kyi dka' 'grel dang grub mtha' spyi'i rnam bzhag cig bka' rtsom mdzad /
lho kha khul rin chen sgang du mkhas grub nor bzang rgya mtsho'i mdun nas dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gyi rtsis cha lag yongs rdzogs dang /
de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dus 'khor spyi don gyi bshad lung sogs dbang bka' mang po gsan /
rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho rang nyid kyis brtsams pa'i drang nges rnam 'byed kyi dka' 'grel sogs brtsams chos mang po spyan lam du phab pas thugs kyi bum bzang gang bas dgyes pa chen por gyur /
slar yang ra sgreng du thengs gnyis pa phebs te bka' gdams pa'i gnas rnams mjal /
gnyal smad nang so rin chen dpal bzang gis gdan drangs pa bzhin gnyal sde drug gi dgon sde'i dge 'dun chig stong tsam 'dus pa'i lung ra chen mo'i gral dbur phebs nas chos bka' zab rgyas bstsal bas dge 'dun kun yid 'phrog par gyur /
nang so tshe dbang pas mthun rkyen sbyar nas tsA ri'i gnas rnams mjal bar phebs /
lho brag khul dang /
rtsed thang /
shel brag sogs la byon nas skya ser mang por mdo sngags kyi chos bka' du ma bstsal te ra sgreng du thengs gsum pa phebs /
re zhig sku mtshams su bzhugs te sgrub pa nyams len mdzad /
de nas dwags po khul du zhabs bcags te sgrom mda' dgon gsar la dga' ldan chos gling zhes ming 'dogs par mdzad /
dgung lo so bzhir phebs pa'i sa sbrul lo la rgyal me tog thang du dgon pa 'debs pa'i re 'dun byung ba bzhin gnas de nyid du zhabs kyis bcags te sa 'dul sogs mdzad /
gtsug lag khang dngos gzhi dang /
gtsang khang sogs khyon ka chen brgyad cu tham pa'i rgya khyon gyi gram bting /
lo de'i dbyar khar 'du khang gi thog yongs rdzogs phub thub pa byung ste dgon der gnas bca' zhing /
chos 'khor rgyal lung rigs smra ba sum brgya'i tshogs rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar mdzad pas kun dga' bas rol bar gyur /
de nas paN chen ye shes rtse mos gzengs bstod kyi zhu yig dang /
bkra shis lhun po'i gdan sar cis kyang phebs dgos pa'i zhu nan byung bar brten /
sngar gyi gnas tshul rnams thugs su ma btags par bkra shis lhun por byon /
gdan sa 'dzin skyong gnang dgos lugs ye shes rtse mos nan gyis gsol rung re zhig tsam las rgyun ring bzhugs rgyu'i thugs mos med pas gnas skabs ring dge 'dun 'dus tshogs nyis stong skor la tshad ma'i gzhung 'chad nyan dang /
bka' gdams glegs bam sogs kyi chos bka' mang du bstsal nas dge 'dun rnams kyi yid kyi shing rta chos kyi nor bus gang bar mdzad de slar yang chos 'khor rgyal du phebs /
dwags kong khul phal cher du phebs nas chos sbyin gyis bkang ba ma zad /
kong po rgya mda' khul du yod pa'i ri kha ba dang /
sang sing dgon gnyis phan tshun ma mthun pa'i 'gal rkyen bsal nas mthun sdebs lugs legs su bskyangs /
slar bkra shis lhun por phebs te gtsang phyogs yul gru mang por chos sbyin gyis tshims par mdzad /
me glang lo la phag gru sde srid ngag dbang bkra shis grags pa dang /
'bras spungs chos rje lha ri pa /
'bras spyi so bcas nas gdan sa 'bras spungs kyi khri la zhabs sor 'khod dgos pa'i gsol ba nan gyis btabs /
lo 'di'i zla ba bzhi par  dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi gdan khrir phebs shing /
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis dus 'da' bar mdzad nas chos sde 'dzin skyong mdzad /
snga sor lha sa'i smon lam chen mo lo ngo brgyad cu gya gsum tsam gyi ring 'bras spungs kho nas 'dzin skyongs thog ser 'bras dge gsum gyi dge 'dun rnams 'du tshogs mdzad bzhin pa de ltar yang /
sa rta lor sde gzar skabs 'bras spungs pa'i sbyin bdag gtso bo sne'u rdzong gi sde srid la yor 'khyom byung rkyen lo ngo nyi shu tsam gyi ring lha sa nye 'dabs kyi bka' brgyud pa dang /
sa skya pa sogs kyi dgon sde'i dge 'dun tshang ma smon lam gyi tshogs la 'gro ba zhig byung yod /
de rjes phag gru sde srid ngag dbang bkra shis grags pa'i srid dbang nyams pa slar sor chud byung ba dang /
lhag par rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i lung rigs kyi yon tan phul du byung ba'i snyan grags dbus gtsang /
dwags kong sogs phyogs gang sar khyab che ba'i dus skabs dang 'phel ba bcas kyis bod sa stag lo nas bzung slar yang 'bras spungs pas smon lam chen mo'i 'dzin skyong mdzad /
gdan sa chen po gsum gyi dge 'dun rnams sngar rgyun bzhin tshogs la phebs /
de skabs 'bras spungs dgon par dge 'dun chig stong lnga brgya skor dang /
se rar dge 'dun sum brgya tsam las med tshod /
lo 'dir phag gru sde srid kyis 'bras spungs rdo khang sngon po rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i bzhugs gnas su sbyor 'jags mdzad /
rten 'brel ched du dga' ldan pho brang zhes pa'i ming btags /
dus mi ring bar se ra theg chen gling zhor 'dzin mdzad rjes grwa tshogs kyang chig stong tsam la 'phel ba dang /
bshad sgrub 'chad nyan yang dar rgyas su song /
lcags glang lor mnga' ris rgyal po 'jig rten dbang phyug pad dkar sde dang /
blon po ngag dbang rnam rgyal gnyis kyis rin po che'i 'bul ba spam mtho ba dang bcas rab byung pa ngang pa'i khyu 'dra ba mang po btang ba la gzhir byas nas btsugs pa'i dgon sde mnga' ris grwa tshang zhes pa de'i ming yang de nas thogs pa yin 'dug dgung lo drug cu re drug tu phebs pa rab byung dgu pa'i lcags glang lor 'bras spungs su zhi ba gshegs /
dad rten dngul gdung rin po che 'bras spungs dgon par bzhugs /
gsung rab kyi rnam grangs ni bstod tshogs skor gyi gsung 'bor chen dang /

zhal gdams skor /

bod ljongs lho kha sa khul 'phyongs rgyas 'phying ba stag rtser yab 'phyongs rgyas sde pa bdud 'dul rnam rgyal dang /
yum yar 'brog sna dkar rtse sa skya dpon chen a len gyi rgyud pa kun dga' lha mdzes gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu pa'i me sbrul lo la sku bltams /

yid gzhung ba /
gzhan la snying rje che ba'i ngang tshul bzang pos dus bda' bar mdzad /
sku rtsed kyi tshul mdzad na'ang chos 'chad nyan gyi tshul dang /
dgon pa 'ding ba sogs kho na mdzad de tha mal gyi spyod pa las rgyang du bsrings /
gzhon nu'i nyams med par thugs sgams zhing brling la dkyel che ba zhig yod /

gsang phu gling smad zhabs drung dkon mchog chos 'phel gnyis kyis ra sgreng jo bo 'jam dpal rdo rje'i spyan sngar brtag zhu mdzad de rgyal ba sku phreng bzhi pa yon tan rgya mtsho'i mchog sprul yin par ngos 'dzin bskyangs /
de skabs dge lugs pa'i sbyin bdag lha btsan dang /
hong tha'i ji /
tsha ba sgang pa dka' bcu ba sogs khams sog gi mi sna rnams nas sprul sku ngos 'dzin gyis gdan zhu zhu phyogs skor skabs de'i dbus gtsang gnyis kyi khrims bdag gtsang pa sde srid phun tshogs rnam rgyal 'das nas lo gnyis song ba dang /
de'i bu karma bstan skyong lo ngo drug las son med stabs der nang blon dbang shugs che ba mgron gnyer bong gong pa dang /
phyi blon sgang zug pa gnyis kyis sprul sku dbus lha ldan du gdan zhu bya rgyur dgag bya'i rgyu mtshan sna tshogs shig phrad kyang /
gdan zhu'i mi sna rnams kyis thabs rnam ci rigs la brten nas /
dbus lha ldan du gdan drang rgyur don du gnyer bas mthar 'bras spungs su khri 'don chog pa'i bka' 'khrol byung ba bzhin /
skyid smad mnyes thang du phyag mdzod bsod nams rab brtan dang /
ser 'bras kyi slob dpon sogs mi sna du mas phebs bsu gzab rgyas dang 'brel chu khyi zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes bco lnga nyin chos sde chen po dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi gdan khrir bkod /
dgung lo brgyad la son pa'i shing byi lor paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan gyis mkhan po dang /
gling smad zhabs drung 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog chos 'phel gyis slob dpon mdzad de dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes /
mtshan ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho 'jigs med go cha thub bstan lang tsho'i sde zhes gsol /
dgung lo bcu gcig thog dga' ldan khri thog so lnga pa 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog chos 'phel yongs 'dzin du bsten te gzhung chen mo bka' pod lnga la phu thag chod pa'i slob gnyer rim bzhin mdzad /
dgung lo bcu drug tu son skabs grwa skor mtshan btags gnang rgyu'i thugs 'dun byung yod na'ang /
phyag mdzod bsod nams rab brtan nas mtshan nyid kho nas ma 'thus pas da dung sku yon gzhan dag mu mthud nas gsan bzhes mdzad dgos lugs gsol ba bzhin mkhar grong chos mdzad kyi sa nas yig gzugs legs par sbyangs thog phyag dpe po ti sum brgya tsam gyi dkar chag legs bsgrigs mdzad /
rje pha bong kha pa dpal 'byor lhun grub kyi drung du zla ba phyed gnyis tsam bzhugs nas /
gsang sngags gsar rnying gi dbang lung khrid man ngag bcas ji snyed cig dang /
'jam dbyangs dkon mchog chos 'phel gyi mdun nas lam rim gyi myong khrid sogs rgya che gsan bsam mdzad /
de rjes paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan gyis mkhan po dang /
las kyi slob dpon gling smad zhabs drung gis mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i bslab sdom bzhes /
mtshan sngar yod thog ngag gi dbang phyug zhes pa kha snon du 'bul bar mdzad /
me glang lor go shri rgyal po bod du 'dzul /
mtsho sngon chog thu sogs kyi dpung stobs bcom nas dge ldan pa'i chos lugs la phan pa chen po bsgrubs pas lha sa'i gtsug lag khang du bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgyal po'i mtshan bzos gnang /
sa yos lor grong smad pa 'phrin las rgya mtshos brtsams pa'i lo 'khor gcig tsam gyi lo tho de'i mchod brjod dang /
lo bshad sogs rgyal ba rang nyid nas brtsams par mdzad pa ma zad /
rtsis rig gi  gzhung lugs nyams pa sor chud kyis gong 'phel 'byung ba'i thabs su dgongs te skar rtsis rig pa sogs la gsan sbyong mdzad pa'i 'go tshugs /
de dang chabs cig rtsis rig la rnam dpyod ldan pa'i mkhas dbang ji snyed cig byon pa'i ya gyal grong smad pa sangs rgyas rgya mtshos phug pa man ngag lugs kyi phyag len gzugs 'gros shin tu rgyas pa'i lo thog zhig brtsams yod la /
'phyongs rgyas pa phun tshogs rnam rgyal gyis kyang bod rtsis lo tho zhig bkod yod pa sogs rgyal ba de nyid kyi sku dus su rtsis rig gi thad la'ang 'phel rgyas che tsam byung bar brten /
phyis lha sa sman rtsis khang gi lo tho'i rmang gzhi bting thub pa byung yod /
lcags 'brug lor go shri bstan 'dzin chos rgyal gyis smar khams be ri don yod kyi dpung sde'i stobs shugs la rgol te pham par byas /
slar yang sog po'i dpung chen bod kyi nub phyogs su 'dzul te lcags sbrul lo gzhis ka rtse yongs rdzogs mtha' bskor nas gtsang pa sde srid dang dmag 'thab zla ba gsum tsam byas kyang gtsang pas mgo ma sgur /
skabs der gtsang pa sde srid la gra sgrig cher med kyang /
stag lung pas go shri phyogs kyi cho bab gnas tshul gtsang par 'phrin bskyal bar brten /
gra sgrig byed pa'i go skabs cung zad byung bar ma zad /
gzhis ka rtse'i mkhar rdzong btsan zhing /
sog dmag gi dmag rgyags dkon pa sogs kyis skabs shig ring rgyal pham gyi dbye ba ma chod /
de rjes dga' ldan pho brang pa'i phyag mdzod bsod nams rab brtan pas dbus phyogs kyi dmag dpung mang tsam zhig sog po'i dpung rogs su btang 'byor gyis phan tshun dmag 'thab snga rjes zla ba dgu tsam byas mthar gtsang pa sde srid karma bstan skyong dbang po 'khor bcas pham /
chu rta lor go shri bstan 'dzin chos rgyal gyis lnga pa chen po'i lung rigs kyi yon tan phul du byung ba'i chos srid kyi mdzad 'phrin la dad pa'i spu long rab tu g.yo bzhin par gzhis ka rtser gdan drangs /
gangs can gyi 'dzin ma'i khyon la gdugs dkar gcig gi khyab pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol te dga' ldan pho brang zhes pa'i srid gzhung thog mar btsugs /

don du dbus gtsang gi mkhas pa yod tshad la brdar sha legs par bcad de bod mi rigs kyi rig gnas bya bzhag thog 'od snang rab tu 'phro ba'i snyan ngag me long gi dka' 'grel dang deb ther dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i glu dbyangs sogs brtsams par mdzad rjes dbu gtsang khams gsum du snyan ngag gi khrid rgyun gong 'phel chen po byung yod /

yum blo bzang chos mtsho gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i sa byi lo sku bltams /
zhag bdun song ba na sku zhang a dge bkra shis bla mkhyen rab 'byams pa'i 'khris su btang bar des lung bstan pa bzhin mtshan bskal bzang rgya mtsho zhes gsol /
li thang chos sde'i srung mas slob dpon mthong ba don ldan gyi yang srid 'khrul med yin lugs kyi lung bsgrags pa sogs gcig nas gcig brgyud kyis dbus gtsang bar du khyab /
skabs de'i bod kyi srid 'dzin lha bzang gis brtag zhib byed po mi sna snga rjes su btang bar brten /
legs nyes ji yong cha ma 'tshal pas byol na legs dgongs te sde dge'i sa phyogs su gdan zhu mdzad /
sde dge'i dpon bstan pa tshe ring nas phebs bsu'i bkod pa bzab rgyas kyis lha lung khung du spyan drangs /
de nas mtsho khri shor rgyal mo'i 'gram sa nas bod sog gi sbyin bdag stobs 'byor che ba rnams kyis gdan zhu byas pa ltar sde dge nas rim gyis btegs /
mi ring bar bstan 'dzin ching wang dpon brgya skor zhig phebs bsur 'byor /
mtsho sngon nye 'dabs a rig chu tshan khar skye bo khri phrag brgal bar mjal kha gnang /
rgya nag nas gong ma'i mi sna 'byor te rgya nag tu phebs dgos tshul bshad kyang mtsho sngon g.yas ru'i dpon khag rnams nas mi sna ched btang gis dgongs zhu byas par brten rgya nag tu phebs dgos ma byung bar re zhig kun dga' nor du bzhugs /
me spre lor kun dga' nor nas chibs thon gyis sku 'bum byams pa gling du phebs /
dge 'dun sum stong lhag gi ser spreng dang /
gong ma'i sku tshab sogs rgya bod hor gsum gyi mi sna du mas bsu ba'i mdzad sgo gzab rgyas mdzad /
de nas chu bzang no min han ngag dbang blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan drung nas sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang sogs gsan pa dang sbrags phyag dpe khag gsan sbyong mdzad /
de skabs gong ma'i mi sna zhig 'byor te khul de'i dpon khag rnams 'dus pa'i sar gong ma'i bka' lung bsgrags don /
tA la'i bla ma'i sprul sku 'dir phebs nas bzungs nged sems shin tu bde /
'di tA la'i bla ma gong ma'i sprul sku 'khrul med yin 'dug nged dang bstan 'dzin chos rgyal gyi gdung rgyud thams cad sbyin bdag yin /
nged nas lo gsum gyi bar du grwa pa brgya dang sum cu so bzhi la dbyar dgun gos rgyu sogs tshang ma 'bul rgyu yin gsungs /
no min han ngag dbang blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan mdun nas thog mar dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa mnos /

de bas dge slong rnams dge sbyor gong 'phel btang na de ga legs zhes phebs /

phangs par gyur pas bstan pa'i zhabs 'degs la dgongs pas dgongs bzhes yong ba nan gyis gsol mthar /

gnas chung chos skyong gi bka' lung /

srid skyong rta tshag gdan sa gsum /
rtse shod drung rigs ser skya spyi mgrin gyi zhu mos bzhin sngar srol gser bum dkrug 'don gyi brtag dpyad ma dgos par 'phral du ngos 'dzin zhus 'thus kyi gong ma'i bka' 'byor /
me glang lor gdan zhu'i mi sna bka' blon g.yu thog gis gtsos gzhung zhabs ser skya du ma zhig dwags po glang mdun du phebs nas gdan zhu bskyangs /
tshal gung thang du paN chen rin po che ched phebs kyis gtsug phud bzhes /
mtshan ngag dbang blo bzang thub bstan rgya mtsho 'jigs bral dbang phyug phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i sde zhes gsol /

sa yos lor de nas spyan drangs te /

dag cha /
go don sogs gsan sbyong legs par mdzad /

lo der paN chen rin po che gshegs pas dgongs rdzogs mchod sprin rgya che bsgrubs /
shing sprel lor sku bcar gzim dpon mkhan po bar zhi ba'i sa nas phyag bris kyi yig gzugs slob gnyer mdzad de mi ring bar yig gzugs phul du byung ba thugs su chud /

mchims mdzod /
'dul ba mtsho TIk dge 'dun grub kyi gsung rgyun par gzhir ma 'khod pa'i kha skong le tshan du ma bcas par gzhi gsar bskrun gyi dbu 'dzugs dang /
zhus dag byed mi sogs bka' bkod bstsal /
shing lug lor yongs 'dzin phur lcog blo bzang tshul khrims byams pa rgya mtshos mkhan slob sbrags ma dang /

bzang gos kyi na bza' /

se ra /
dga' ldan bcas so sor chibs bsgyur thog mkhas mang rgyu skar gyi phreng ba 'khrigs pa'i dbus su grwa skor dam bca' chen mo'i mdzad sgo khag legs par bskyangs /

bla sprul khag dang /

dbu phar /

gzur gnas mkhas mang dgyes pa dang /

gor+Sha rgyal khang nas gsol ba btab pa ltar /
phyogs der rgyal bstan nyin mo'i snang ba gsar du spel phyir rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che glegs bam cha tshang bsgril rdzas rang 'grigs bka' rgya dang sbrags rtse drung ser smad 'phrin las bstan pa rdzong bda' mdzad /
lcags byi lor rab byung bsnyen rdzogs sogs bstan pa'i rtsa ba so thar gyi sdom rgyun spel ba'i mkhan po'i bya ba mdzad pa'i skabs su babs pa'i thog ma tshe mchog gling sprul sku dang /

bsam yas /
gnas chen tsA ri'i rtse skor sogs la gnas gzigs su chibs bsgyur thog dgon sde khag gi rten mchog spyi'i spyan sngar mchod sprin tshar du dngar ba 'bul gshoms dang /
dge 'dun rnams la bsnyen bkur mang 'gyed /
skye bo ser skya du mar chos kyi 'khor lo rgya che bskor bar mdzad pa sogs bzhed don lhun gyis grub ste slar dbus ljongs lha sar zhabs sor 'khod /

ring min pho brang nas btegs te mtsho khar sbyin bdag rnams la mjal 'phrad dang 'don chos kyis tshim par mdzad /
de nas khams kyi gdan sa rnams su byon nas dad ldan rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te re zhig bzhugs /
ring po ma 'gyangs par dbus lha ldan du chibs kha thengs bzhi pa bsgyur nas /
rgyal dbang lnga pa dang /
mthon por gnas pa'i yon gyi bdag po rnams la skyes 'bul dang mjal phyag zhus par gzigs skyong dgyes tshor tshad med bstsal /
jo shAka rnam gnyis sogs rten rnams la mchod 'bul dang /
ser 'bras gsum gyi dge 'dun gyi sde rnams la bsnyen bkur rlabs chen po sogs rnam dkar gyi mdzad 'phrin rgya che'i ngang nas re zhig bzhugs /
slar yang lnga pa chen por dgongs pa zhus nas khams kyi gdan sa rnams su phebs /
gdan sa'i grwa rigs dang yon bdag tshang ma chos dang zang zing gis tshim par mdzad /
khyad par dpa' shod dga' ldan rnam rgyal pho brang rten dang brten par bcas pa 'gran pa'i zla thams cad dang bral ba de nyid gsar du bskrun cing rab gnas dang /
dga' ston gyi rim pa legs par mdzad /
khong gi sku rabs kyi phreng ba ma lus pa pho brang 'di nyid du zhabs kyis bcags shing /
thos bsam sgom gsum gyi sgo nas rgyal ba'i bstan pa spel ba'i 'phrin las kyi 'od stong 'gyed pa'i bsti gnas mchog tu gyur /
de nas gong ma chen po'i bka' bzhin ma hA tsi na'i yul du chibs kyi kha lo thengs gnyis pa bsgyur /
rgya nag pe cing du gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos dbyings su thim pa'i tshul bstan /
gong ma nas dgongs rdzogs kyi chos sprin rgya cher spros shing /
slob ma'i tshogs kyis kyang dgongs rdzogs byed pa'i rnam dkar gyi dge ba 'byams klas pa bsgrubs /
khong gi 'das lo dngos ni /
khong gi skye 'phreng blo bzang dpal ldan rgyal mtshan sa byi lor 'khrungs par dpags na /
khong dgung lo lnga bcu nga lngar phebs pa /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i me mo phag gi lor 'das pa yin nam snyam par dpyad /

... byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i brgyud pa gsum gyi bla ma rnams la gsol ba 'debs cing nges 'byung byang sems yang dag pa'i lta ba rgyud la skye ba'i 'dod gsol dang bcas pa chos kyi sgo 'byed ces bzhugs so / /
... bla ma'i rnal 'byor bka' drin nges gsob sogs bzhugs so / /

mkhan chen dpal ldan snyan grags pa'i drung du dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa zhus /

chab mdo /

khri steng mdzes pa'i bu chen bzhi'i nang tshan stag phu gu shri dpal ldan don grub ni rab byung drug pa'i chu khyi lo la /
lho kha khul gong por skyo rigs su sku bltams /
gzhon nu'i dus nas stag phu dpal ldan rin chen mdun rab tu byung /
byang sems r+wa sgreng pa /
'jam dkar ba /
rgyal tshab dar ma rin chen sogs mkhas pa'i dbang po du ma bsten nas /
mdo sngags rig gnas kyi gzhung lugs rgya mtsho lta bur gsan sbyangs mdzad /
rje tsong kha pa'i spyan sngar bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa mnos /
dgung lo nye gsum par /
lha sa skyid chu shar kha'i stag phu chos sde'i gdan sar phebs /
skabs der khong la gu shri chen po zhes mtshan snyan grags che bar gyur /
dpal 'bar rdzong gi nub ngos dang kong po rgya mda'i shar ngos dang nye ba'i byang sta ri 'go bde chen chos 'khor gling gi dgon pa btab /
de nas rim bzhin kong po rgya mda'i khul gyi nyang po lha ru dgon sogs gzhis dgon 'ga' yang zhor 'dzin mdzad /
dgung lo gya lngar phebs pa rab byung brgyad pa'i me pho khyi'i lor zhi bar gshegs so / /
khong gi gsung ni /
nged dpe mdzod khang du thor bu phyogs bsgrigs byas pa pod gcig bzhugs yod / /

stag phu gar dbang blo bzang chos kyi dbang phyug gi gsung 'bum / /
... bris ma /
... ca chags ru 'od gsal sgrub sde'i jo bo rin po che'i sku brnyan mthong grol chen mo'i dkar chag ngo mtshar 'bras bus brjid pa'i yongs 'du'i 'khri shing zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun ma yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgo nas zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bya tshul bdud rtsi'i 'od dkar zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... shing byi zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes brgyad la khal kha'i mi sna gzim 'gags sogs kyi gdong skyabs mgon rje btsun dam pas bka' 'dri gnang ba'i lan du phul ba sogs dris lan 'ga' zhig bzhugs / /
... bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i dpal mgon chen po lcang skya ye shes bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por zhabs brtan phul skabs maN+Dal gyi bshad pa'i zin bris bzhugs / /
... 'jam mgon bstan pa'i gsal byed bse sprul pa'i sku rin po che'i 'khrungs rabs sku thang rgyas pa 'bri tshul bzhugs / /
... rnga chen zhes pa chu pho khyi'i lor g.yag khrab ri bo mdangs ldan gyi bde mchog sgrub mchog par mchod thebs nyams gsos bgyis pa'i spyi khra 'dod 'byung dpag bsam ljon pa zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... shug thang dgon 'jigs byed dkyil chog par zhal 'debs bgyis pa'i spyi khra khyad par bzhi ldan  zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gtsug gtor rnam par rgyal ma'i stong mchod brtan bzhugs sogs phan bde snang ba'i dga' ston gyi sgo nas byed skabs kyi lag len zin thor bkod pa bzhugs so / /
... sbud mda' rnam rgyal dpal 'bar gling du 'khor lo sdom pa dril bu zhabs lugs lha lnga'i dkyil chog gsar 'dzugs bgyis pa'i spyi khra 'dod 'byung gter gyi bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
...  bla ma'i rnal 'byor legs tshogs lhun grub ces bya ba dang gzhan yang bla ma'i rnal 'byor gsol 'debs sogs bzhugs so / /
... tshe dpag med kyi tshe sgrub ngag 'don 'khyer bde sogs gsol 'debs smon tshig 'dod gsol 'ga' zhig bzhugs so / /
... ston pa dus kyi 'khor lo rje rin po che sogs bla ma rnams la gsol ba 'debs cing 'don bya'i don la smon pa dgos 'dod kun 'byung dngos grub dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... kun gzigs rgyal dbang yab sras kyi 'khrungs rabs mdor bsdus gsol 'debs smon tshig dang bcas pa bzhugs so / /
... bstan pa'i gsal byed no yon ho thog thu ye shes don gnyis lhun grub kyi 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs nor bu'i 'phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ser 'dam dbu ma stag rtser grags pa'i gzhi bdag bsangs mchod bkra shis dpal ster bzhugs / /
... bka' rgyud 'phel rgyas gling gi rgyab mdun gyi gzhi bdag gi bsangs mchod bkra shis dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  dga' ldan rab brtan gling gi gzhi bdag spu rgyal sogs kyi bsangs mchod 'dod rgu'i dpal ster  zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dga' ldan 'phel rgyas gling gi bsrung ma rdo rje rdzing btsan chen por gser skyems 'bul tshul mnga' gsol bcas bzhugs / /
...  mgon po trak shad 'khor bcas drag tu bskul ba rngam pa'i sgra dbyangs dang de nyid kyi mnga' gsol bcas bzhugs / /
... lha mchog tshangs pa chen po'i tshogs mchod mdor bsdus bzhugs / /
... ar sdoms su grags pa'i gzhi bdag gi bsangs mchod 'dod rgu'i dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gzhi bdag 'bong nga g.yu mdog tu grags pa'i bsangs mchod phan bde'i 'bras ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal ba thod dkar gyi gnyer gtad bzhugs so / /
... bla ma'i rnal 'byor mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... skyang khyim jo bor grags pa'i gzhi bdag gi bsangs mchod bzhugs / /
... mi tra brgya rtsa nas 'byung ba'i rdo rje phag mo nag mo lha lnga'i sgrub thabs snying po bsdus pa bde chen myur lam zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... snga 'gyur bstan pa'i gsal byed nyi grags mchog sprul rin po cher zhabs brtan rten 'byung gi maN+Dal 'bul ba'i bshad pa 'chi med sgra dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs / /
... gser gdung khang sogs kyi snyan dar zhal byang bzhugs so / /
...  'jigs byed kyi phyag mtshan sogs kyi zhib cha /
... me stag lor gsol dpon tA bla ma'i gdong byang phyogs bstan 'gro'i gtsug rgyan khal kha rje btsun dam pa rin po che nas bka' mchid ring 'tsho'i rten 'byung dang 'brel ba gnang ba'i lan du phul ba'i zhu 'phrin rma bya dga' ba'i zlos gar bzhugs so / /
... me stag lor nyi grags sprul pa'i sku rin po che phebs gdong sde dge zhe chen rgyal tshab pa nas snyan ngag gi lam nas drangs pa'i 'phrin yig byung ba'i lan snyan tshig dri bsung 'thul ba'i puN+DA ri ka'i me tog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dben gnas dge 'phel byang chub gling bka' gdams chos kyi pho brang gi sngags pa brjod pa'i rab tu byed pa dpyid kyi me tog gsar pa'i do shal zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bka' gdams chos kyi pho brang gi gtsug lag khang rten dang brten par bcas pa bzhengs pa'i dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngo ba'i smon tshig tshogs gnyis 'dzad pa med pa'i rgya mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bka' gdams chos kyi pho brang gi 'khor chen dkar chag zin bris bzhugs / /
... bla ma sangs rgyas byang sems kyi bstod tshogs zhabs brtan gsol 'debs bden tshig smon lam gyi rim pa phyogs gcig tu bkod pa bzhugs so / /
... rnga chen zhes pa chu pho khyi'i lo stag gdong ri bo dpal 'bar gyi 'jigs byed dkyil chog mchod thebs nyams bsos bgyis pa'i spyi khra 'dod 'jo'i 'khri shing zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  lhag pa'i lha mchog rje btsun ma seng lding nags kyi sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs dngos grub kun 'byung bdud rtsi'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  bris ma /
... kha dam pa gong ma'i 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs rgyas pa ngo mtshar padma dkar po'i chun po ltar gyi thang bkod dwangs shel me long bzhugs so / /
... dam pa gong ma'i 'khrungs rabs phan bde'i ljon pa bskyed pa'i sa bon nang ltar gyi sku thang rgyas par bri tshul gyi thang bkod bzhugs / /
... 'jam mgon bstan pa'i sgron me sgrub khang sprul pa'i sku rin po che'i 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs brtan bzhugs smon tshig dang bcas pa lhag bsam 'dab ma rgyas pa'i pad dkar zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rnam 'dren bstan pa'i gsal byed rgya ston sprul pa'i sku rin po che blo bzang 'jam dpal don 'grub kyi 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs brtan bzhugs smon lam dang bcas pa mi 'gyur yongs 'du'i 'khri shing zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bstan pa'i gsal byed khri dwags sprul pa'i sku'i 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs smon tshig dang bcas pa dge legs 'dab brgya bzhad pa'i smon lam zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bstan pa'i gsal byed jo bo bla ma bskal bzang dge legs rgyal mtshan gyi skyes rabs gsol 'debs dad pa'i kun da bzhad pa'i zla zla zer zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bstan pa'i gsal byed rdza ra lo sprul sku blo bzang bstan pa'i dngos grub kyi 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs don gnyis lhun gyis grub pa'i dga' ston ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das dpal dus kyi 'khor lo la rten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  bla ma dang gsang ba'i bdag po dbyer med pa'i rnal 'byor zab mo dngos grub 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bla ma'i rnal 'byor bzhugs so / /
... zab lam bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs myur 'jug sogs bla ma'i rnal 'byor rim pa rnams bzhugs lags so / /
... bla ma rgyal ba sras bcas kyis phyag mchod cho ga'i sgo nas bsags sbyangs kyi gnad bsdus pa bya tshul thar pa'i 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mi tra brgya rtsa'i nang tshan 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed gdong drug lha nyer gcig pa'i sgrub thabs dngos grub 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... kun rig rnam par snang mdzad kyis cho ga shin tu bsdus pa ngan 'gro'i tsha gdung sel ba'i kar du ra zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs seng+ge sgra'i sgrub thabs phan bde'i bsil sbyin zla ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs mdor bsdus gtan bde'i legs tshogs lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... 'phags pa thugs rje chen po phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs mdor bsdus bzhugs so / /
... thugs rje chen po rgyal po lugs kyi sgo nas ma Ni ril sgrub bya tshul byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i snying po zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das ma rnam par rgyal ma'i sgrub thabs mdor bsdus 'chi med mchod stsol ces bya ba  bzhugs so / /
... rgyal chen rnam thos sras kyi lha dpal gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi sgrub thabs dngos grub kun 'byung zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... bde mchog gi sgo nas tshogs mchod shin tu bsdus pa bya tshul bzhugs so / /
... dpal 'khor lo sdom pa dril bu lugs gtso bor gyur pa'i yi dam gyi sgo nas lho sgo'i cho ga bya tshul mdor bsdus nyams thag dbugs 'byin gdung sel zla 'od ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lha sna tshogs kyi sbyin sregs kyi zin bris thor bu bzhugs so / /
... dpyod ldan mgu ba skyed pa'i 'phrin yig gi rim pa tshangs pa'i sgra dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rmad du byung ba'i gtam gyi sbyor ba 'chi med lha'i rnga bo che'i sgra dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dge slong byams pa bskal bzang gi dris lan bzhugs so / /
... tha ma kha'i nyes dmigs mdor bsdus bkod pa bzhugs so / /

... mgon chos lha mo gsum gyi sgo nas bka' bsgo bya tshul bar chad kun sel zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyal ba'i bstan bsrungs chen po 'ga' zhig gi rten thugs bskyed chog bzhugs so / /
... rgyal ba'i bstan bsrungs chen po rnams la las bzhi'i 'phrin las 'chol tshul dngos grub myur 'gugs rdo rje'i sgra dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  chos bsrungs rnams kyi gtor 'bul gser skyems bskul 'phrin bcol rten 'dzugs kyi 'dod gsol sogs kha thor sna tshogs kyi skor bzhugs so / /
... dpal ye shes kyi mgon po gur lha brgyad ma'i mngon rtogs bskangs bshags bstod bskul dang bcas pa dngos grub kyi rgya mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon po lho nub pa'i mngon rtogs bskangs bshags bstod 'phrin dang bcas pa bdud dpung kun 'joms zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... gnubs lugs dpal mgon stag zhon gyi mngon rtogs bskangs bshags bstod 'phrin dang bcas pa 'phrin las myur mgyogs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... tshogs bdag mgon po seng zhon gyi mngon rtogs bskangs bshags bstod 'phrin dang bcas pa 'phrin las myur 'gugs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal ye shes kyi mgon po phyag bzhi pa gtso 'khor la bsangs mchod 'bul tshul ma hA kA la dgyes pa'i mchod sprin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rin chen mang sprul rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi bsangs mchod dngos grub char chen 'bebs pa'i sprin gyi rnga gsang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mthu stobs kyis dbang phyug dam can rdo rje legs pa /
mgar ba nag po gtso 'khor gyi gtor chog bskang bshags bstod bskul dang bcas pa dpa' bo'i sgra dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... myur mdzad ye shes mgon po phyag drug pa'i bka' sdod gtso bo gnod sbyin chen po k+She Ta pA la'i gtor chog 'phrin las myur 'grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... legs ldan beng chen gyi bka' sdod gtso bo bdud mgon nag po stobs chen la mchod gtor  'bul tshul 'phrin las lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mgon po chos rgyal lha mo rnam sras gnas chung bse khrab pa grags rgyal ma g.yu sgron zhang paN bcas kyi gtor chog mdor bsdus 'phrin las lhun grub ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... stag gdong ri bo dpal 'bar gyi gnas bsrung dge bsnyen rdo rje klu btsan gyi gtor chog bskang bshags bstod bskul dang bcas pa 'dod 'jo'i dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rta lha sde lnga'i bsangs mchod bkra shis dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... thab lha'i bsangs mchod mi gtsang nyes sel zas bcud 'dod rgu'i dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... klu dung skyong dkar po'i rten 'dzugs bya tshul phan bde'i mchog sbyin zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mdo khams sde dge rdza chu kha'i gzhi bdag rdza rgyal rdo rje 'phel phyug tu grags pa'i gsol mchod bkra shis dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... lha gnyen chen po jo bo kong lha rdo rje 'bar ba rtsal gyi bsangs mchod dge legs 'dod pa 'jo ba'i bum bzang zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mdo khams chab mdo'i bye brag yul dga' 'dzom zhes pa'i gzhi bdag gi bsangs mchod bkra shis dbyangs snyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

...  rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... stag phu gar dbang chos kyi dbang phyug gam /
mtshan gzhan blo bzang chos kyi dbang phyug ni /
dus rabs bco brgyad pa'i dkyil te /
bod rab byung bcu gsum pa'i dus kyi mi yin la /
khong gi gdan sa ni /
byang nag chu dang nye bar sngon blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis btab pa'i dgon pa dge phan byang chub gling zhes pa de yin /
khong gis rtsa ba'i bla ma rgyal sras bskal bzang thub bstan gtsos /
klong rdol bla ma /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po sogs bla mar bsten nas /
mdo sngags rig gnas kyi gzhung lugs mang por gsan bsam mthil phyin mdzad cing /
zab khrid dbang lung rjes gnang sogs kyang shin tu mang po zhus /
rgyud sde rnams kyi dgongs don zab dgu rgya cher bkrol ba la zla bral gyi gdeng thob /
khal kha'i rje btsun dam pa lta bu bla chen rnams nas kyang gzhung don dka' gnad 'dri ba'i slob dpon du bsten /
sku tshe phal mo cher bcad mtshams bzhugs pa sogs nyams len bsnyen sgrub kho na mdzad /
thub sku mthong ba don ldan /
gsung rab glegs bam brgya phrag ma Ni dung 'khor che legs sogs sku gsung thugs kyi rten khyad 'phags rgya che bzhengs /
yul de'i skye 'gro yongs la chos char 'bebs /
gsung rab du ma gcig tu bsdus pa'i dbu med bris ma pod che legs shig nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs yod / /

stag phu padma badzra'i gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... khyab bdag stag phu ba chen po padma badzra'i gsung las /

...  khyab bdag stag phu ba chen po padma badzra'i gsung las /
zhal gdams gsung mgur gyi rim pa phyogs gcig tu sdebs pa tsit+ta ma Ni'i do shal bzhugs so / /
... sgrol ma seng ldeng nags sgrol la brten pa'i rlung gnon man ngag shin tu zab pa bzhugs / /
... khyab bdag stag phu ba chen po padma badzra'i gsung las /
tshogs 'khor gyi rim pa phyogs gcig tu sdebs pa grub gnyis 'dod rgu'i rgya mtsho bzhugs so / /
... rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i nyams len gyi cha lag zab mo bdud kyi gcod yul mkha' 'gro'i snying khrag bzhugs so / /
... khyab bdag stag phu ba chen po padma badzra'i gsung las /
mchog dman mgron la bsangs dang gser skyems 'bul tshul dang /
'phrin bcol /
snyan dar smon tshig sogs kyi skor phyogs gcig tu sdebs pa kun bzang bdud rtsi'i sprin 'phreng zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... yang gsang gnas mchog mkha' 'gro snying rdzong mchod yul dmigs gsal du bgyis pa'i mchog dman mgron la bsangs mchod bya tshul bde legs rgya mtsho'i dpal 'bar zhes bya ba bzhugs  so / /
... gnas mchog yang gsang mkha' 'gro snying rdzong la bsangs mchod 'bul tshul bde legs dpal 'bar zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... yang gsang mi shigs thig le 'bar ba'i gnas chen por bsangs mchod 'bul tshul phun tshogs rab rgyas zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... ma chags lhun grub gnas yul chen po ru /
bzhugs pa'i rtsa gsum lha tshogs gzhi bdag bcas /
mchod tshul thun min snga 'gyur lugs ltar bzhugs /
dam nyams 'gro ba'i yul min snying gi rgya / /
... rgyal chen sku lnga'i gtor bzlog gi bca' bsgrig zin bris bzhugs so / /
... gnas dgon ri bo dpal 'bar gyi chos sde'i srung ma /
padma'i dge bsnyen rdo rje klu btsan gyi thugs dam rgyas par bskang ba'i rim pa bzhugs so / /
... gnod sbyin brel phongs can mnan chog bzhugs so / /
... kun 'dus padma lha rtse'i gnas yig skal ldan re skong bzhugs so / /
... khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha'i sprul sku rin po che'i 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs bai DUr+ya'i phreng ba dang /
sku tshe'i bar chad zhi ba'i gsol 'debs le tshan dang /
khang gsar rdo rje 'chang gi 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs /
grib khrus bya tshul /
g.yu sgron ma'i gser skyems bcas bzhugs so / /
... gar gyi dbang phyug bzhi pa'i 'khrul 'byams gsang ba'i lo rgyus rgya can skor bzhugs so / /
...  rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... stag phu padma b+dz+ra ram rig 'dzin padma lhun grub ni rab byung bco lnga pa'i me pho byi ba lo la 'khrungs /
sku gzhon nu'i dus nas stag phu sprul skur ngos 'dzin byas nas sbyor sdeb blor 'dzin sogs kyi dbu btsugs /
yongs 'dzin du ma'i mdun nas zab dgu'i man ngag thob /
mdo sngags rig gnas sbyong ba'i gzhi legs par btsugs /
dgung lo bcu gsum pa sa pho byi ba'i lor zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes gnyis kyi snga dror 'bras spungs su mjal skor phebs /
rten khyad 'phags dang /
gsung rab rnams la phyag mchod dang /
pha bong kha pa byams pa bstan 'dzin /
bka' 'gyur ba thub bstan chos kyi dbang phyug sogs la dbang rjes gnang zhus /
dgung lo sum cu par bod yul gyi gnas chen mtha' dag tu gnas mjal phebs /
dgung lo so gsum par bka' gdams pho brang du blo bzang thub dbang la lam rim gyi myong khrid zhus /
dgung lo so dgu par dbus ri la bar skor phebs /
myang phug tu bcad rgya bgyis /
dgung lo zhe drug par /
gsang sngags dpal gyi sgrub sde gsar du bzhengs /
bum gter sbas pa dang rab gnas mdzad /
mdor na dbus kyi gnas chen tshang mar chos mjal phebs shing /
gdul bya mang por chos sbyin rgya cher spel /
dgon rten gsar bzhengs sogs rnam dkar gyi bya ba rgya cher mdzad cing /
spyir dge ldan ring lugs 'dzin pa'i sprul sku zhig yin yang rgyal ba lnga pa ltar nang na gsang sngags rnying ma'i lugs gtso bor mdzad do / /
ngag sgros ltar na dgung lo re lnga re drug tsam la 'das sam snyam par dpyad mdzod /
gsung ni bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi gsol 'debs /
gsung mgur zhal gdams /
cho ga'i skor dang gsang rnam bka' rgya ma bcas /
chos tshan rnams ka kha'i go rim bsgrigs pa lha sa'i par ma pod chung zhig nged dpe mdzod khang du bzhugs so / /
...ka kha...  @# / /

... stag phu yongs 'dzin ye shes rgya mtsho'am /
mtshan gzhan chu bzang bla ma yang grags pa de ni /
spyi lo'i dus rabs bco brgyad pa'i dbus tsam la /
bod dbus kyi sa cha kong po'i yul du sku 'khrungs /
khong  dbus stod lung nyang bran chu bzang ri khrod du yun ring por rnal 'byor la brtson bzhin bzhugs pas /
chu bzang bla ma zhes dang /
nags shod stag phu sprul sku gar gyi dbang phyug gi yongs 'dzin mdzad myong bas stag phu yongs 'dzin zhes grags /
sku na phra ba'i dus nas ser smad thos bsam nor bu'i gling du grwa sar zhugs te gsan bsam mdzad /
de mo no min han thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtsho /
mtshan zhabs mkhan po tshe dbang bsam 'grub sogs mkhas shing grub pa thob pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen du ma bsten nas /

dbang lung rjes gnang man ngag sogs kyang dpag tu med pa zhus /
ring po ma 'gor bar sde snod gsum dang /

byis pa'i ming don grub tshe ring btags /

dgung lo bdun par phebs dus a khu yang rang yul du log phu nu sogs kyang cher skyes /
khong ma smad la'ang 'tsho ba legs tsam byung nas yi ge 'bri klog dang 'dzin skyor sbyong ba'i dbu tshugs /
a khu bla ma yin stabs byis pa 'di rab byung byas na legs tshul smras kyang /
yum gyis khyim gzhis 'dzin 'jug dgos bsams nas rab byung byed du mi 'jug sbyor sdeb blor 'dzin sogs la yun ring tsam 'gor /
dgung lo bcu gnyis par ma drin can lnga pa'i lam du gshegs /
'chi kha'i kha chems su rab byung byed chog pa'i gnang ba thob /

ming blo bzang rab brtan gnang /

de nas chos spyod phal cher blor 'dzin mdzad /

de nas mi ring bar spyi khang gsar skrun gyi las grwa btsugs /

tA la'i brgyad pa'i yongs 'dzin dka' chen ye shes rgyal mtshan sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen du ma bsten nas dbang lung man ngag mang po zhus shing /
khyad par klong rdol bla ma'i mdun du tha snyad rig gnas kyi skor snyan ngag sum rtags sogs la'ang sbyangs pa mthil phyin mdzad /
de ltar legs par bshad pa'i gsung rab rgya mtsho lta bur thos bsam yun du mdzad nas thugs kyi bzhes pa yongs su gang ste ded dpon rgya mtsho'i gling nas log pa ltar dgyes bzhin par rang yul phyir phebs /
a lag sha'i g.yon dgon mi pham chos  gling ngam dge sgrub gling du 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi dbu tshugs /
khong ni rig pa'i gnas kun phyogs brgyar spel ba la lhag bsam bzang po do zla bral ba zhig yin stabs /

rdo rams pa lha zhe'i mdun du /

pe cing yung dgon du byon nas dad ldan rnams la chos sbyin bstsal cing /
ja mchod 'grel pa rtsom pa'i dus su ja'i 'byung khungs skor rgya yi gzhung lugs mang por thugs dpyad mdzad /
khong sku tshe shin tu yun ring bzhugs yod pa 'dra ste <blo sbyong don bdun ma'i gtam theg mchog nye lam> ni dgung lo gya gcig tu phebs pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i sa phag lor brtsams 'dug khong dgung grangs brgyad cu lhag bzhugs ring dus tshod skad cig tsam yang chud zos su mi btang bar 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la 'bad pa lhur len mdzad cing /
dus tshod stong zad du btang nas le lo rnam g.yeng ngang nas mi tshe 'khyol thabs byed mkhan dag la dgag pa nan min mdzad pa ni khong gi gsung <bslab bya'i mi chos dga' ston> du mi tshe phyed ni gnyid la g.yur bas khyer / /
de phyed bza' btung g.yos su bya bas chod / /

zhes gsungs pa las shes nus so / /
