...tha... rigs dang dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag rje btsun blo bzang chos kyi nyi ma'i gsang gsum rmad du byung ba'i mdzad bzang 'dab brgya'i dga' tshal gyi cha tsam gtam du byas pa rtogs brjod pad ma dkar po'i smad cha bzhugs so / /
... dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po blo bzang chos kyi nyi ma'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rnam par thar pa puN+Da ri ka'i 'khri shing zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... dgon lung byams pa gling gi sprul sku thu'u bkwan chos kyi nyi ma ni /
kan su'u zhing chen khongs su pho rod lang gru'i yul gyi bye brag phun tshogs lung par /
pra yi rus nas brgyud pa'i yab dbang skyabs rgyal dang /
yum ba ri bzang chos mtsho skyid gnyis kyi sras su /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i me mo sbrul lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bdun gyi snga dror sku bltams /
dgung lo drug pa bzhes pa'i skabs su /
dpon po bstan 'dzin chos 'phel sogs dgon lung du 'byor nas grwa pa rnams dang gros bsdur thog dogs pa yod pa'i bu chung bzhi khong dang bcas lnga char gyi ming dang rigs rus sogs bris nas /
pe cing lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje dang dga' ldan khri sprul gnyis la phul /
bla ma rnam gnyis kyis gnas tshul 'di lha sar tA la'i bskal bzang rgya mtsho la gsung brtags kyi zhu 'phrin phul /
gsung brtags kyi lan ma 'byor ba'i sngon du 'brog phrug cig thu'u bkwan pa'i yang srid du ngos bzung nas /
thu'u bkwan gong ma'i dbon po rnams kyis thog ma'i rten 'brel yang bsgrigs /
'on kyang thu'u bkwan dngos slob blo bzang mkhas mchog sogs kyi thugs la gtan nas ma babs /
mi ring bar pe cing nas lcang skya dang khri sprul gnyis kyis lang gru'i pra sti dbang skyabs rgyal gyi bu thu'u bkwan gyi sku skyer thag bcad pa'i bka' shog dang /
tA la'i bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i lung brtags bcas 'byor bas /
dgon lung nas thu'u bkwan gong ma'i dbon po ngag dbang dge legs dang /
hor dum chos rje sogs dpon g.yog mang po lang grur sprul sku gdan 'dren du 'byor /
nyer mkho'i yo byad dang na  bza' sogs gya nom pa phul /
dgung grangs drug pa chu khyi'i lo'i zla ba drug pa'i tshes bzhi'i nyin lam du zhugs /
phebs lam kun tu bsu ma rim pa mang po 'byor /
de nas dgon lung du 'byor na nye ba na /
ngur smrig 'chang ba'i dge 'dun nyis stong lhag gis ser sbreng gzab rgyas kyis bsus te thu'u bkwan bla brang du gdan drangs /
thu'u bkwan ngag dbang chos kyi rgya mtsho'i gdan khrir bkod /
lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje'i bka' ltar dmar tshang dbon chung blo bzang chos 'dzin klog gi dge rgan du bsten /
sbyor klog rnams dka' tshegs med par mkhyen /
chos bzang ri khrod dang /
dgon lung gi rgyab ri'i brag rtsa'i gzim khang gnyis su res mos kyis bzhugs te dpe 'dzin sogs la 'grus par mdzad /
dgung lo dgu par chos bzang ri khrod kyi dbyar gnas su tshogs la phebs cing cho ga'i zhal 'don tshang ma mthar phyin /
dgung lo bcu gcig pa me yos lor /
sum pa ye shes dpal 'byor gyi drung du rab tu byung /
de nas dgon lung gi chos grwar zhugs te /
tshad ma'i gzhung rnams gsan pa'i dbu btsugs /
lo gnyis tsam la rigs lam che 'bring chung gsum sbyangs zin nas tshad ma'i skor la shin tu byung bar gyur /
dgung lo bcu gsum par lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje pe cing nas mdo smad du phebs par chibs bsur phebs /
lcang skya dgon lung du phebs skabs /
thu'u bkwan bla brang du gdan drangs te dngos 'bul rgya chen dang bcas khong gi mdun nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes bzhi la lcang skya pe cing du phebs bskyod mdzad /
zla ba bcu gcig par 'brum nad shin tu lci ba byung yang yun mi ring bar dwangs /
dgung lo bcu bzhi pa nas tshogs dbus su phebs shing thub pa'i skyes rabs so bzhi pa'i bshad pa mdzad /
phar phyin thugs gnyer byed pa'i mgo btsams /
zhor du snyan ngag sdeb sbyor /
skar rtsis sogs tha snyad rig gnas skor la'ang dpe klog mang du mdzad /
sum pa mkhan por dam chos mang po zhus /
dgung lo bcu drug par yab dgung grangs don bzhi pa 'das rjes /
dgung lo bcu bdun par yum 'das te skyo bas mnar zhing /
yab yum gnyis la dge rdzogs rgya che bsgrubs /
lo der rang yul gyi zhwa dmar dgon du phebs /
lung rjes gnang mang po gnang /
dgon pas 'bul nor gya nom pa bstabs /
khong gis kyang tshe dpag med kyi li sku khru tshad ma gtsos rten dang mang 'gyed rgya che gnang /
dgung lo bco brgyad pa sa khyi lor dgon lung nas gong mar lha ldan du phebs rgyu'i zhu ba phul /
ston khar gong mas dbus su phebs chog pa'i gser yig gnang ba 'byor /
de 'phral sum pa mkhan po'i spyan sngar bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa mnos /
dgung lo bcu dgu pa sa mo phag gi lo zla ba lnga pa'i nang du dbus gtsang chos kyi chol khar chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur /
dgon lung nas thon nyin par dge 'dun bgres gzhon tshang mas gling 'dabs bar skyel ma byed /
chibs kha lan gsum bsgyur ba sogs myur mjal gyi rten 'brel bsgrigs /
dgon pa dang bla brang gi las sne rnams kyi rgya sgo'i bar bskyal /
de nas byang lam brgyud de dbus lha sar 'byor nyin bka' blon bzhi'i sku tshab dang /
'bras spungs dang sgo mang sogs kyi bsu ba byas te /
dpal grub khang tshan du bzhugs /
phyi nyin par po ta la'i pho brang du tA la'i bskal bzang rgya mtsho mjal /
de nas mi ring bar 'bras spungs su phebs te  bkra shis sgo mang gi chos grwar zhugs /
'jam bzhad 'jigs med dbang po dge rgan du bsten /
nyin shas mtshams su phur bu lcog tu phebs nas /
ngag dbang byams pa mchog dang mjal /
chos 'brel zhu zhing tsong kha pa'i sku brnyan dang 'jam dbyangs gser thang zhig gnang nas slob sbyong nan smin dgos pa'i bslab bya mdzad /
de nas gzhung chen mo rnams la thugs brtson lhod med mdzad /
dgung lo nyer gcig pa me glang lor tA la'i bskal bzang rgya mtsho dgongs pa rdzogs par /
skyo ngal chen pos gdung mjal du phebs te dngul srang lnga bcu sogs kyi mchod thebs phul /
lo de'i zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bco lnga nyin phur lcog ngag dbang byams pa'i drung du bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa zhus /
'di ni bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa blang ba thengs gnyis pa yin /
lo 'dir tsha ba'i nad drag po zhig gis btab nas zla ba gcig lhag tsam bsnyungs /
de nas rim gyis nad las grol /
de nas mi ring bar lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje dbus su phebs pa mjal zhing /
bka' chos mang po zhus /
dgung lo nyer gsum par tA la'i yang srid ngos 'dzin byed pa'i ched du paN chen dpal ldan ye shes lha sar phebs pa mjal /
lcang skya dang lhan du dus 'khor gyi dbang zhus /
skabs der sde pa gzhung nas zhwa lu gser khang gi gdan sa 'dzin dgos pa'i bka' rgya phebs /
lcang skya'i zhal gsung ltar zhwa lu'i gdan sa skyong bar mdzad /
de nas gtsang phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur te rgyal rtse brgyud dpal 'khor ches sde'i sku 'bum chen mo sogs mjal ba brgyud bkra shis lhun por byon /
paN chen 'jal kha zhus shing bka' bslab mang po zhus /
sa skya bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros lhar sar phebs 'dug pa gsang stabs kyis mjal bar phebs /
des rkyen byas te sa skya dgon chen du byon nas bdag chen rin po che mjal zhing zab chos 'ga zhus /
gtsang gi dgon sde khyad par can rnams su mjal skor phebs rjes slar yang bkra shis lhun por paN chen rin po cher thon phyag zhus /
zhwa lur phebs te gdan khrir bzhugs /
gtsug lag khang dang rten rnams mjal zhing mchod sprin rgya cher spros /
dgung lo nyer lnga pa lcags sbrul lor mdo smad du tshur phebs la nye ba na /
gzhung nas tham ga che chung /
na bza' /
rta dar 'bog lcag sogs chen por 'os pa'i gzengs bstod dang /
bstan pa'i gsal byed no mon han zhes pa'i chos lo gnang /
snye thang du tA la'i bdun pa'i sprul sku mjal bar phebs /
rtsa ba'i bla ma phur lcog ngag dbang byams par thon phyag zhus rjes /
bla ma dang 'bral mi phod pa lta bus spyan chab dbang med shor bzhin par gzim shag phyir thon /
de nas gzhung nas gnang ba'i mkhan chas rnams spras te mdo smad du byon /
sum pa mkhan po gtsos skya ser stong phrag 'gas bsu ba dang bcas dgon lung du 'byon /
tshogs par mang 'gyed sogs legs par btang zhing rdo bcal du nyin gsum ring dam bca' bzhugs /
sum pa mkhan chen sogs kyis bstod pa mdzad /
lo de'i zla ba bcu gcig par dgon lung gi gdan khrir bzhugs /
las sne gsar bskos /
chos 'chad nyan sogs mdzad /
khrir bzhugs nas lo phyed gsum tsam ste dgung lo nyer bdun pa chu lug lor gong ma chen lung nas pe cing du phebs dgos pa'i gser yig gnang ba 'byor /
'jam bzhad 'jigs med dbang po dgon lung gi khrir phebs /
zla ba gnyis  pa'i mjug tu dgon lung nas bteg phebs byams la bzhugs nas dmag mi bcu gnyis kyi srung ma dang bcas zhag lnga bcu la pe cing du 'byor /
lha khang ser por bzhugs /
nyin de rang la lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje gsang stabs kyis mjal kha zhus /
dgyes pa chen pos gsung lhug par bstsal /
mi ring bar pho brang nang mar gong ma chen por 'byor phyag la phebs /
gong mas rang gi bzhes 'phro'i na bza' dang /
hu thog thu chen por 'os pa'i gsol ras bdag rkyen mdzad /
har chin wang rat+na sid+d+hi yis sog yul du gtan drangs nas dam chos mang po zhus te /
'bul nor shin tu rgya chen phul /
ston mjug pe cing du tshur 'byon /
rjes nas lo re bzhin dbyar khar sogs yul du 'gro don mdzad par phebs te gdul bya rgya cher thel /
dgung lo sum cu pa me khyi lor sa chu ma 'phro ba'i rkyen gyis sku gzugs cung ma bde yang skyon chen ma byung /
zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes gsum nyin par /
gong mas khong la jing si'u chan zhi hu thog thu zhes pa'i mtshan snyan dang /
dngul gyi tham ga chen po sogs gnang /
mtshan de'i don bod skad du rnam dag bslab ldan bsam gtan gyi slob dpon 'phags pa chen po zhes pa'i don no / /
skabs der gong mas kau shri'i go gnas gnang rgyu'i bka' phebs /
gong ma'i lugs la ti shri /
kau shri /
chan shri gsum ni gong ma'i slob spon gyi gnas su bkur pa'i mtshan yin /
dgung lo so gnyis pa sa byi lo'i zla ba dang por gong mar thon phyag zhus te rang yul du phebs pa'i sta gon mdzad /
gong mas dngos po'i gsol ras gya nom pa bstsal /
pe cing gi dgon sde khag gi bla chen tshang mas skyel ma mdzad /
sog po'i wang mang po'i re zhus ltar sog yul kun tu zhabs kyis bcags /
dam chos spel ba /
dge tshul slong gi sdom pa 'bogs pa sogs rnam dkar dge ba'i legs mdzad rgya cher sgrub bzhin par lo de'i zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu gnyis la dngos po'i 'byor ba rgya chen po dang bcas rang gi gdan sa dgon lung byams pa gling du 'byor /
chu bzang sprul sku dang sum pa mkhan chen gtsos pa'i bla chen rnams la skyos ma'i 'bul dngos gya nom pa dang /
dgon pa'i dge 'dun par mang ja dang 'gyed legs par gnang /
khyad par 'jam bzhad 'jigs med dbang po gdan drangs te dgon pa dang rten gsar rnams la rab gnas mdzad cing /
'jam bzhad la nor bu'i rigs sna tshogs /
gos dar sku chas /
mchod chas rin thang bral ba sogs 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul /
'du khang zhig gso dang mgon khang gsar skrun /
nang rten mang po gsar bzhengs /
gsung rab mang po brtsams pa bcas lo gsum lhag tsam dgon lung du bzhugs /
dgung lo so lnga pa lcags yos lo der gong mas pe cing du 'byon dgos pa'i gser yig 'byor bar brten zla ba lnga pa'i tshes lnga la rang dgon nas bteg sog po'i yul gru brgyud do lon no'ur du lcang skya dang rje btsun dam pa mjal /
de nas zla ba brgyad par zhe hor du phebs nas gong ma mjal /
der gong mas po ta la'i pho brang ltar gyi dgon pa gsar du bzhengs pa la lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje /
sog rje btsun dam pa /
khong yab sras gsum gyis rab gnas dang smon lam gyi tshogs dbu mdzad /
gong ma rang yang tshogs su phebs nas rnam pa gsum la 'bul ba spam mtho ba dang /
grwa pa stong lhag la sku 'gyed gya nom pa btsal /
de nas sogs yul gyi  dgon sde tshang mar phebs /
khu re dgon du zhag gsum bzhugs /
dgung lo so drug pa 'brug lo'i zla ba dgu par dgon lung du tshur 'byor /
dgung lo so bdun pa chu sbrul lo'i dgun khar bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du 'jam bzhad nas gdan zhus ltar phebs /
tshogs par dam pa'i chos kyi dga' ston spel /
mkhas mang mgu ba'i rkyen gyis bsngags brjod mdzad /
dgung lo zhe gcig pa me bya lor /
gong ma'i ma yum thes hu gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs bsngo smon gong ma'i dgongs bzhed ltar bsgrubs /
dgung grangs zhe gsum pa sa phag lor /
phyag mdzod dbon don grub dbang rgyal g.yog 'khor dbus su gtong sgo 'bul du mngags /
tA la'i blo bzang 'jam dpal rgya mtsho /
paN chen dpal ldan ye shes sogs la 'bul chen /
jo shA ka sogs rten khyag 'phags la phyag mchod rgya chen phul /
skabs der paN chen dpal ldan ye shes rgya nag tu phebs lam der brgyud /
khong 'bri chu'i bar bsu bar byon /
paN chen dgon lung du gdan drangs te /
dam chos kyi dris lan mang po mdzad /
paN chen sku 'bum du yun ring bzhugs dus khong yang paN chen mdun bzhugs nas gang cir bka' bgros mang du mdzad /
byi ba lo'i zla ba gsum par paN chen rgya nag tu phebs /
lo de'i zla ba bcu pa'i mjug tu paN chen pe cing du dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i gnas tshul gsan /
thugs skyo ngal shin tu chen po mdzad /
dgung lo zhe bdun par dgon sde thar pa gling rten dang brten par bcas pa gsar bzhengs grub cing dngul 'gro srang chig khri lhag tsam btang /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa 'jigs med dbang po sogs gdan drangs te rab gnas rgyas pa mdzad /
zla ba bzhi par 'jam bzhad dbus su phebs par phebs skyel zhus /
zla ba der gong ma'i bka' las /
thu'u bkwan hu thog thu zla ba brgyad pa tshun la tsha byol pho brang du sleb par gyis zhes phebs /
tshes brgyad la gser yig pa dgon lung du 'byor /
zla de'i tshes nyi shu nyin rgya nag tu phebs /
sog yul brgyud zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes bdun la zhe hor du bkra shis lhun po'i lha khyang du gong mar mjal kha zhus /
nyi shu bzhi la pe cing du 'byor /
zla ba dgu pa'i tshes gcig la lcang skya ri bo rtse lnga nas pe cing du phebs pa mjal /
nyin shas rjes sog yul du phebs /
lo gnyis lhag ring sog po wang dang bla ma mang po'i re 'dod bskangs /
dgung lo lnga bcu pa rta lo'i zla ba bcu gnyis par dgon lung du 'byor /
dgung lo nga gcig pa me lug lor /
zla ba gnyis par sbyin bdag gtso bo khar chin wang rat+na sid+d+hi ri bo rtse lngar 'das pa gsan /
thugs skyo ba'i ngang dge rdzogs dang bsngo smon rgya che bsgrubs /
mtsho sngon gyi sku 'bum sogs dgon sde yongs la phebs /
dgung lo nga gnyis pa sa sprel zla ba dang por chu bzang du lcang skya sprul sku mjal bar phebs /
de rjes bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du phebs nas 'jam bzhad dang chos kyi bgro gleng mdzad /
dgung lo nga gsum pa sa bya lo'i zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bzhi la sku 'bum dgon pa'i gdan khrir bzhugs /
bya khrung gi khri pa dgongs zhu mdzad de 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa bzhugs rgyur thag bcad nas zla ba drug par 'jam bzhad khrir bzhugs /
dgung lo nga lnga pa lcags phag lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes gnyis la 'jam bzhad 'jigs med dbang po ka mdo ru sku gshegs pa'i gnas tshul gsan /
tshes drug la ka mdor phebs /
thugs skyo ngal  tshad med ngang phyag 'tshal zhing sprul sku myur 'byon gsol 'debs ljags rtsom mdzad /
pe cing nas gong mas rgya nag tu phebs dgos pa'i bka' phebs kyang thabs mkhas kyis byol /
sku 'bum du bzhugs nas 'chad nyan dang dbang skur rjes gnang sogs mdzad /
sku 'bum gyi khri thog lo gsum bzhugs te lcags phag lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bdun nyin mkhan khri dgongs pa zhus /
khri pa gsar pa gro tshang mkhan po bskos /
rang nyid dgon lung du phebs /
dgung lo nga brgyad pa shing stag lo'i zla ba dang por chos bzang ri khrod du bcad rgya mdzad nas bzhugs /
dgung lo nga dgu par chu bzang du phebs nas lcang skya mchog sprul rgya nag tu phebs grabs la mjal 'phrad dang phebs brdzangs zhus /
'jam bzhad sprul sku ngos 'dzin gyi don du bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du byon /
zla ba bcu par sog yul du phebs nas yon bdag wang rnams kyi zhe 'dod skong bar mdzad /
lo gcig tsam 'gor /
dgung lo drug cu pa'i lo smad la dgon lung du tshur phebs /
dgung lo re gnyis pa'i me sbrul lo zla ba gsum par bkra shis 'khyil du 'jam bzhad sprul skur mjal 'phrad du phebs /
tshes bcu la mchog sprul rin po che'i gtsug phud bzhes te rab byung gi sdom pa bstsal /
zhabs brtan gsol 'debs brtsams /
de nas rim gyis dgon lung du tshur byon /
dgung lo re gsum pa sa lug lo'i zla ba dang po pe cing du gong ma chan lung gnam du gshegs pa'i gnas tshul 'byor /
zhag nyer gcig ring dgon lung du dgongs rdzogs bsgrubs /
dgung lo re bzhi pa'i zla ba bzhi par sku 'bum du skor tsam byon /
zla ba bdun par dgon lung du byon rjes sog yul du phebs /
lo gnyis tsam ring chos sbyin bstsal /
dgung lo re drug pa chu khyi lo'i zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu bdun nyin dgon lung du 'byon /
skabs der snyung gzhi bzhes nas yun ring song /
rim gro sman bcos yun ring byas kyang ma phan par /
rab byung bcu gsum pa'i chu khyi lo zla ba drug pa'i tshes pa bcu'i nyin gyi phyi dror dgon lung byams pa gling du sku gshegs so / /

mdo smad the bo rong gi yul du dred lung ya re zhes bya ba'i grong sder /
yab dpal tsha shes rab bzang /
yum thar bza' sngo long ma gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i me mo yos kyi lo1687zla ba bcu pa'i tshes gcig nyin pa'i snga dror sku bltams /
dgung lo bdun par khu bo blo bzang bkra shis kyi mdun du klog slob pa'i dbu btsugs /
lo gcig lhag ring sbyor klog blor 'dzin sogs la 'bad brtson mdzad /
dgung lo brgyad pa shing khyi lor rang yul 'brum nad kyis khyab par brten /
'brum nad las byol zhor pha khu spun zla dang lhan cig phrag dkar gnas chen 'jal bar phebs pa'i lam bar brag dgon bla ma bstan pa dar rgyas 'jal /
phyag dbang gnang zhing rab tu byung na legs zhes gsungs /
dgung lo bcu gnyis pa sa stag lo'i ston khar brag dgon bla ma bstan pa dar rgyas drung du rab byung dge tshul gyi sdom pa blangs /
ngag dbang smon lam zhes pa'i chos ming bstsal /
dgung lo bco lnga bcu drug pa gnyis la slob dpon ngag dbang bstan 'dzin mdun nas /
yig dkar nag 'bri ba dang lha ris bcas sbyangs /
dgung lo bcu bdun par slob dpon ngag dbang bstan 'dzin dang lhan du 'bum gling bar du gnas chen dang dgon khag rnams su mjal skor phebs /
tshur lam co ne dgon dang chos rdzong gi dge 'dun 'dus  sde mjal zhing smon lam btab /
de nas rim gyis gsung rab klog pa sogs la thogs pa med par gyur te grong du gsung rab klog pa sogs kyi dkor rgyug kyang thengs 'ga' phebs /
dgung lo bcu dgu pa shing bya lo nas lo gsum bar mos po bla rgan rtsar grong chog 'chad nyan mdzad de bzhugs /
dgung lo nyi shu pa sa pho khyi lo'i ston khar mkhas mchog chas pa zhabs drung mdun nas bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa mnos /
dgung lo nyer brgyad pa shing pho rta lo'i zla ba lnga pa'i yar tshes la sgar chen grogs mang dang bsdebs nas dbus lha ldan du byon /
thog mar 'brog ri bo dga' ldan rnam rgyal gling du phebs /
de nas lha sa'i dgon sde /
rten khyad 'phags /
gnas chen rnams su mjal bar phebs /
skabs der tA la'i drug pa tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho'i sku tshab /
'gro mgon ye shes rgya mtsho bzhugs yod kyang rgyu mtshan 'ga'i rkyen gyis mjal stabs ma bde /
gtsang la phebs nas paN chen blo bzang ye shes lan gnyis mjal /
khong gi spyan sngar bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bskyar bsgrub zhus /
ming zhig gnang rogs zhus pas blo bzang bsam gtan zhes bya ba bstsal /
bkra shis lhun por zla ba phyed ring bzhugs nas khres po khur nas zhabs thang du lha sar tshur phebs /
dbus gtsang du zla ba brgyad tsam las ma 'gor bar mdo smad du tshur 'byor /
dgung lo nyer dgu pa shing lug lo'i zla ba dang por nye gnas 'jam dbyangs rgya mtsho dang 'grogs te a mo bka' chen mjal bar phyin /
zla ba phyed gnyis ring bka' chos zhus /
de nas ju nang du tA la'i bskal bzang rgya mtsho mjal bar phyin /
rigs gsum mgon po bsnyen lung gnang zhing thugs dgyes pa chen pos rjes su 'dzin /
dgung lo sum cu pa me sprel lo'i zla ba gnyis par yang a mo chos rje mjal bar phyin /

dge ldan rnam rgyal gling dgon pa btab /
gnas der bkra shis chos rdzong zhes pa'i ming btags pa'i yul gru sa yi dge dgu yongs su 'dzom pa rtse gzhung zhes pa'i sa cha ni khong gi 'khrungs yul yin /
sa der sngon sog dmag 'dzul nas bzung /
mdo stod smad dang dbus gtsang bcas su sog o rod rgyal po gu shri bstan 'dzin chos rgyal gyi rgyud pa rnams kyis mi rabs 'ga'i bar dbang bsgyur byas /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i chu mo yos kyi lor ching dmag gis bstan 'dzin wang btul rjes sog po'i dbang bsgyur bsgyel yang mtsho sngon gyi sa mang por sog rigs mang po lhag yod stabs /
drung chen shes rab rgya mtsho'i rigs rgyud kyang yab no'i kho dang /
yum tsi na thar rnam gnyis sog rigs yin zhing /
bod rab byung bcu gsum pa'i chu mo phag gi lo la rtse gzhung khongs kyi brag dmar mdor sku 'khrungs /
gces par bskyangs nas dgung lo drug bdun la phebs pa na /

dbu can /
dbu med /
skungs yig sngags sogs sbyor klog phun sum tshogs par gyur /
rgya gar lany+tsa dang wartu /
ang yig mkha' 'gro'i brda yig dkrugs yig sna tshogs bcas la thogs pa med par mdzad /
da dung ka ra'i yi ge /
nai pa la'i yi ge hor yig gsar rnying rnams kyang sbyangs /
mdor na yig rigs sna tshogs 'bri klog la 'gran zla bral ba byung /
dgung lo bdun bzhes pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i sa mo sbrul gyi lor 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa sku thog gsum pa blo bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtsho dbus phebs gra sgrig gi ched du sbyin bdag so sor 'byon bzhud gnang /
dpon sa ching wang gis gdan 'dren zhus te rtse gzhung du phebs /
sku zhang bla mas khong 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i mdun grwa rgyun du phul /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pas dgyes tshor chen pos grwa pa legs po 'ong zhes pa'i bka' lung dang bcas phyag mdud bstsal /
de nas bzung rings par bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du grwa sar 'gro rgyu'i thugs 'dun rgyun du 'khrungs /
bla brang dgon du bzhugs pa'i gung thang bstan pa'i sgron me'i snyan pa thos pas /
lus ba spu g.yo zhing mig mchi ma 'khrugs pa'i dad pa 'khrungs /
dgung lo bcu drug pa sa pho stag gi lor sog po'i tshong 'grul rnams dang 'grogs te zla ba bcu pa'i tshes 'gor bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du 'byor /
zla de'i tshes brgyad la rdo rams pa dkon mchog dge 'dun gyi drung du tshangs spyod dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa dang rab byung gi sdom pa zhus te ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan bzhes shing sangs rgyas bstan pa'i sgor zhugs /
tshes bcu bdun nyin bla brang bkra shis 'khyil gyi grwa tshang bzhi'i ya gyal thos bsam gling grwa tshang gi chos grwar zhugs /
dge ba'i bshes gnyen dkon mchog don yod slob dpon du bsten nas bsdus grwa sbyangs /
dgung lo bcu bdun pa sa mo yos kyi lo'i zla ba dang por gung thang bstan pa'i sgron me'i spyan sngar dge tshul gyi sdom pa mnos /
mtshan dkon mchog bstan 'dzin zhes pa bstsal /
gzhan yang 'jam bzhad blo bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtsho /
dkon mchog bstan pa'i sgron me /
sde khri 'jam dbyangs thub bstan nyi ma /
dpal mang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan /
rgyal mkhan po grags pa rgyal mtshan sogs mkhas dbang bcu phrag gsum la nye bar bsten nas /
dbang rjes gnang lung  khrid man ngag mang po zhus /
mdo sngags gzhung lugs mang por gsan bsam rgya chen mdzad /
bsod grags sprul pa'i sku dkon mchog rgya mtsho'i phyag g.yog byas nas thag nye ring mang du phebs /
bla mas skabs 'gar bka' bkyon phyag 'bebs mdzad na'ang gus pas 'khur /
skabs shig bsod grags rin po che dang khong dpon slob 'brog phyogs su phebs dus shig la /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'ang der bzhugs yod pa mjal /
'jam bzhad gzim gur nas phyir byon te bsod grags la /
!!khyod kyi grwa pa bstan 'dzin 'di /
grwa pa legs po /
rnam dpyod dang go rgya can snyan dang gas sogs rig gnas la mkhas pa /
yon tan can zhig red 'dug nga la da lta yig mkhan bzang po med pas 'di gar bsdad na rung ngam+'+'+g+sungs /
bsod grags pas kho rang 'thad na los chog zhus /
de nas 'jam bzhad sku phreng gsum pa'i drung yig gi 'gan bzhes /
bka' shog dang springs yig sogs phyag bris gang dgos yod tshad chad lus med par khong gis bris /
'jam bzhad pas drung yig gzhan dag gis bris pa rnams la bcos bsgyur mang po mdzad kyang /
khong gis bris pa rnams la thugs gting nas dgyes shing /
a khu bstan 'dzin gyis bris pa la bcos bsgyur ga la dgos gsungs nas bcos bsgyur mi mdzad /
dpal mang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi drung du rgyal tshab rje'i tshad ma'i brjed byang chen mo dang tshad ma mdo tshad ma sde bdun sogs tshad ma'i dpe cha rnams la sbyangs pa mthil phyin mdzad /
dgung lo nyi shu par rdo rams pa dkon mchog dbang phyug sogs las phar phyin skor gsan /
gdan sa'i yig cha mtha' dag gzigs thog bod kyi mkhas pa gong ma'i dgag sgrub kyi rigs pa'i 'gros tshang mar thugs dpyad zhib tu mdzad /
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dgongs don thugs su chud /
lo bzhi'i ring sbyangs te dgun chos steng phar phyin gyi grwa skor mdzad pas /
dge bshes mang pos bsngags brjod mdzad /
dgung lo nyer bzhi par dbu ma'i gzhung lugs sbyong ba'i dbu tshugs slob dpon klu sgrub kyi rigs tshogs drug dang /
dpal ldan zla ba'i dbu ma 'jug pa gtsos dbu ma'i skor gyi gzhung lugs mang po /
gung thang bstan sgron dang /
dpal mang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan bcas las gsan cing /
lta ba'i skor la dgongs pa zab mo 'khrungs shing rtsa sher zhal 'don rgyun 'khyongs mdzad /
dgung lo nyer drug par mdzod kyi 'dzin grwar zhugs /
mngon pa mdzod rtsa 'grel rgya bod la grags pa mtha' dag gzigs par ma tshad /
rje 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i phyag phyir sku 'bum du byon skabs /
yig tshogs dbus su mon grwa pa tshul khrims bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i mdzod 'grel mjal bar brten /
yang yang dpyad cing 'dris par mdzad /
mdzod kyi dka' gnad mang po'i dogs mdud grol /
dgung lo nyer brgyad pa lcags stag lo'i zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad la /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa blo bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtshos mkhan po dang /
lha rams pa blo bzang chos 'dzin gyis gsang ston /
klu shod pa blo bzang dkon mchog sogs kyis las slob bcas mdzad de bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa blangs /
mkhan pos khong la mtshan shes rab rgya mtsho zhes gnang /
de nas 'dul ba lung sde bzhi dang mdo rtsa sogs 'dul ba'i skor gyi gzhung lugs rnams la gsan sbyong mdzad /
gzhan yang gsang sngags rgyud sde bzhi'i gzhung rnams dang /
rig gnas  thun mong ba sgra dang snyan dngags rtsis bcas gung thang bstan sgron dang rgyal mkhan chen sogs las gsan /
bzo'i skor rnams a mchog sprul sku 'jam dpal sprin rgya mtsho dang /
gcu 'khor sngags rams pa bcas las gsan /
mdor na rig pa'i gnas che chung kun la sbyangs pa mthar phyin mdzad pas shes bya gang la'ang thogs pa med par gyur /
chos grwar bzhugs dus 'tsho ba ngan ngon la brten nas brtson 'grus shugs drag mdzad pas /
dpal mang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan nas!!khyod kyis zas nor ha cang blos btang drag 'dug+'+'+ces bkyon par mdzad /
bla brang dgon pa'i bla slob rnams kyi re skul dang /
sde khri rin po che'i dgongs pa ltar dus 'khor grwa tshang du rnam snang mngon byang gi sgrub mchod cha lag dang bcas pa gsar du btsugs /
mdo sngags kyi gzhung mang 'chad cing /
'don rta dbyangs thig rdul tshon tshun chad zhib par bslabs te bstan pa spel ba'i bya ba rgya cher bsgrubs /
dad ldan slob ma rnams kyis phul ba'i dkor nor yod tshad dge 'dun par mang 'gyed dang /
'du khang gi rten gtso zhal thang rnams kyi mtha' gsham dang zhal khebs /
'du khang bzhi'i nang du rje blo bzang grags pa'i sku re bzhengs /
tshogs chen 'du khang du jo bo'i sku /
phyag dpe dang zin shog lhag ma rnams kyang bsod grags rin po cher phul zhing /
sgyu ma'i dngos por zhen chags gtan nas bral /
sku 'da' la nye ba na /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pas dbus gtsang la gtong sgo mdzad rgyu'i zhabs 'debs su dngul srang chig stong phul /
khong las zab chos gsan pa'i zhal slob /
'jam bzhad sku thog gsum pas gtsos /
bla sprul mang po dang /
mkhan slob dge 'dun bla brang bkra shis 'khyil na yod pa dang /
dbus gtsang khams hor bcas nas byon pa dpag tu med cing mkhas grags kun tu khyab par gyur /
khong ni dbus gtsang sogs grwa sa gzhan du phebs ma myangs kyang bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du thos bsam sgom gsum dang /
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis sku tshe 'da' bar mdzad cing /
rig par bya ba'i gnas kun la mkhas pas slob ma bla sprul mkhas pa mang po spel /
gsung rab kyang shin tu mang po brtsams te bod kyi rig gnas mi nyams gong 'phel du 'gro ba la byas rjes bsub tu med pa bzhag yod /
rnam thar dngos ma mjal bas nam sku gshegs pa ni zhu thabs bral lo / /
khong gi gsung tshang ma khyon bsdams na pod nyi shu tsam yod skad kyang /
mngon sum par du 'khod pa ni po ti bdun yod 'dug cing /
nged dpe mdzod khang du khong gi gsung /
brjed byang dang zin bris sna tshogs /
rtogs brjod dang sku brnyan gyi lo rgyus /
tshogs gtam dang bslab bya'i skor bcas pod bdun po cha tshang yod / /

thub bstan chos kyi grags pa ni /
mdo khams byang rgyud sde dge'i yul gyi sa skya bla ma zhig yin /
spyi lo'i dus rabs bcu dgu pa'i stod tsam ste bod rab byung bcu bzhi par 'khrungs /
khong ni chen po'i go sar gnas pa'i bla sprul lta bu min zhing /
grwa dkyus ma zhig yin yang /
sku gzhon nu'i dus nas rab tu byung ste /
zla bral mkhas dbang dam pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang po rtsa ba'i bla mar bsten cing /
de min gyi mkhas grub du ma slob dpon du bsten nas rig pa'i gzhung lugs rnams la gsan bsam rgya cher mdzad /
khyad par 'dul ba'i bslab gzhi yongs rdzogs dang /
byang sems kyi sdom pa'i skor rnams thugs sbyong nan smin mdzad /

spyod 'jug 'grel chen zhig kyang ljags brtsams mdzad /
so thar gyi sdom pa mig 'bras ltar bsrungs shing ltung ba'i nyes pa phra mos kyang ma gos  par ma zad /

khong gis rgyun gyi spyod lam gang 'dra zhig bstod cing dang du len pa dang /
gang 'dra zhig smod cing dor bar mdzad pa ni khong gi gsung <<blo sbyong bdud rtsi'i snying po>> las!!spyod lam kun tu rang gi sgo gsum la / /

a mdo mdzod dge dgon gsar dga' ldan rab rgyas gling gi dge bshes shig yin /
'khrungs gshegs kyi lo tshigs dang rnam thar da phan lag tu ma son cing /
khong gi gsung rtsom nang kun mkhyen sku phreng gsum pa 'jigs med rgya mtsho'i dus mchod kyi bshad pa dang /
kun mkhyen sku phreng bzhi pa skal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug khri la phebs pa'i brtan bzhugs kyi bshad pa yod par ma zad /
gzhi gsum gyi nyams len gsar du tshugs pa'i smon lam zhig gi mdzad byang du /
rab byung bco lnga pa'i chu spre lo  la brtsam tshul gsal ba bcas la brtag na /
khong ni 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa sku phreng gsum pa'i sku tshe'i ring dang /
sku phreng lnga pa sku gzhon nu'i bar du bzhugs yod par gsal bshad byung /

yi ge 'bri klog 'don chog yig cha /

lnga pa chen po'i sku mdun du bcar /
lnga pa chen po dang zhang po sde srid 'phrin las rgya mtsho rnam gnyis mdun nas /
yi ge'i sbyor klog rtsis dkar nag sgra snyan ngag bzo dang gso ba /
nang don rig pa bcas sbyangs pas rig par bya ba'i gnas kun la thogs pa med par gyur /
lnga pa chen po dang zhang sde srid nas chab srid 'dzin skyong gi bslab ston yang mthil phyin mdzad par brten /
yun mi ring bar chos srid lugs zung la mkhyen pa mkha' ltar yangs shing /
bod mi rigs dang /
bod kyi rig gnas 'dzin skyong spel gsum byed par lhag bsam zla dang bral ba thugs la 'khrungs /
khong dgung grangs nyer bdun du son pa sa lug lo zla ba drug pa'i tshes drug nyin par lnga pa chen pos khong sde srid du bskos thog bca' yig phyag rjes kyis brgyan pa bstsal te bod ser skya tshang mar shes su bcug bca' yig 'di ni da lta po ta la'i sum skas mgor bris pa de yin /
sde srid sngon ma ltar srid kho na 'dzin pa min par lnga pa chen po'i bka' ltar chos dang 'jig rten kun la bla ma'i rjes 'dzin  legs par mdzad /
khong sde srid kyi go sar bzhugs nas lo lnga'i bar lnga pa chen po 'tsho zhing bzhugs yod stabs /
chos srid gang thad lnga pa chen por bslab ston zhus /
btsugs nas ring por ma lon pa'i dga' ldan pho brang gi srid dbang sra brtan dang 'thus tshang bar mdzad /
gtsang pa sde srid skabs kyi khrims yig la gzhir bzung nas <<khrims yig zhal lce bcu gnyis pa>> zur rgyan dang bcas gtan la phabs /
sa skya 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa'i dus kyi chen por 'os pa'i las tshan bcu gsum du grags pa de nyid 'phel rgyas su btang ste srid 'dzin sde khag gi las khungs khag mang btsugs /
las khungs de dag gi byed sgo'i rnam grangs zhib gsal 'khod pa'i bca' khrims sgrig yig <<blang dor gsal bar ston pa'i dwangs shel me long>> zhes pa gsar du brtsams /
bod khul rdzong gzhis khag gi 'bangs mi'i them tho zhib bsher dang /
rdzong gzhis gnad che chung gi rim pa'i khyad par /
yul thon la dpag pa'i khral bsdu'i gzhung yig gsar bkod thog yong 'bab sdud mkhan dang /
dpya khral sdud po bkar rgya ba sogs gsar pa bskos /
sa gnas gal che'i rigs la chos rdzong zung 'brel gyi srid dbang lam lugs gsar du btsugs /
las khungs so sor rtag par bskor g.yeng zhib 'jug sgo nas chos srid 'phel thabs la thugs brtson mdzad /
dbus gtsang dwags kong sogs su mi dkyus ma'i zol gyis chos srid bskyangs tshul la 'bangs khrod kyi gleng brjod ji yod rtog zhib tu phebs pa sogs mkhas mdzangs ldan pa'i bya ba rgya chen mdzad /
la dwags rgyal po seng gi rab brtan gyis tshur rtol gyi dpung tshogs lhags pa tshar gcod pa'i ched du /
dga' ldan tshe dbang dpung tshogs bcas pa mngags te dgra sde tshang ma pham par byas shing /
mnga' ris skor gsum slar yang chab 'og tu bcug sde srid dgung grangs sum cur phebs pa chu khyi lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes nyer lnga la lnga pa chen po dgongs pa chos dbyings su thims /
skabs der khong sde srid kyi go sar bzhugs nas lo bzhi dang zla ba brgyad tsam las phyin med cing /
de snga chos srid gang cir bla mar bka' bslab zhu chog kyang /
da ni chab srid kyi 'khur 'gan yongs rdzogs khong gi phrag par babs /
sku na phra zhing nyams myong mang po med stabs /
lnga pa chen po 'tsho bzhugs skabs ltar lag len thub min the tshom gyi dra bas bcings /
de'i thog skabs der bod du sog po'i dbang shugs kyang che tsam btsan bsdad byas yod par brten /
lnga pa chen po sku gshegs pa la khag btags nas /
bsam yul las 'das pa'i gnas tshul mi yong ba'i don du /
lnga pa chen po sku gshegs pa'i mtshan mo de rang la /
dge slong 'jam dbyangs grags pa /
mchod dpon ngag dbang shes rab /
drung 'tsho dar mo pa /
chang khyim ngag dbang mkhyen brtse sogs nang 'khor nyung shas gros la bkugs te bsam gros bskur /
tshang mas bla ma'i zhal chems ltar gnas skabs gsang rgya dgos par thag bcad /
thabs du mar brten nas lo bcu bzhi tsam gyi bar gsang rgya mdzad /
dgung grangs so brgyad pa lcags rta lor 'dzam gling du snyan grags kyi yongs su khyab pa'i rtse pho brang dmar po rten dang brten par bcas pa bzhengs pa'i dbu btsugs /
dgung grangs zhe gsum du phebs pa shing phag lo'i bar lo drug la yongs su grub ste rab tu gnas pa mdzad cing gser gdung rin po  che'i dkar chag <<mthar gling rgya mtshor bgrod pa'i gru gzings>> zhes pa brtsams /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i chu mo bya lo la /
gong ma khang shis nas gser gyi byang bur bkod pa'i go sa'i bka' yig dang /
!!rdo rje 'chang tA la'i bla ma'i chos srid 'dzin cing rgyal ba'i bstan par dar rgyas su skyong ba'i sa dbang tham ka'' zhes pa'i gser tham gnang /
tA la'i lnga pa'i yang srid brtsad gcad pa'i ched du gsang ba'i sgo nas chos rje zil gnon rdo rje dang /
sde pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan sogs dbus gtsang stod smad kun tu mngags /
mon yul du tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho lnga pa'i sku skye yin par thag bcad /
gnas skabs ring sding pa che ngag dbang snyan grags kyi yang srid yin pa'i zol gyis mtsho sna rdzong du gdan drangs nas bzhugs su bcug dgung lo zhe bzhi pa me byi lor gsang rgya yongs su bkrol te bod kyi ser skya tshang mar lnga pa zhing du gshegs tshul dang /
yang srid thag chod zin pa sogs gsal bar bsgrags /
rgya nag gong mar yang snyan seng phul /
phyi lo'i zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bzhi nyin par tA la'i lnga pa'i sprul sku yab yum dang bcas pa sna dkar rtse'i gzim chung bstan 'dzin pho brang du gdan drangs /
paN chen blo bzang ye shes kyang der phebs nas /
sprul skur rab byung gi sdom pa phul /
mtshan blo bzang rin chen tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho zhes gsol /
zla ba bcu pa'i tshes nyer lnga nyin par rten 'brel gzab rgyas dang bcas tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho dgung grangs bco lngar phebs pa de nyid po ta la'i gser khrir mnga' gsol /
rgya nag gong mas ched brdzangs gnang ba'i lcang skya ngag dbang chos ldan gyis gong ma'i bka' shog rten dang bcas phul te che 'don zab rgyas mdzad /
lnga pa'i dgongs rdzogs la dmigs nas se 'bras dge gsum gyi dge 'dun khri phrag brgal ba nyin bcu'i ring smon lam chen mo 'tshog rgyu'i tshogs mchod gsar du btsugs /
bod zla gnyis pa'i tshes sum cu nyin mchod rdzas kyi rnam grangs stong phrag brgal ba thogs pa'i dge 'dun mang pos gtsug lag khang nas rim byon gyis po ta la dang ra mo che'i gtsug lag khang bcas yongs su bskor ba'i tshogs mchod ser sbrengs kyi dus mchod gsar btsugs thog sgrig yig <<byang chen nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor>> zhes pa gsar du brtsams /
lha ldan gtsug lag khang gi bar khang dang rtse thog gi khang stong rnams la lha khang dang /
skor lam shar byang gi 'chi med lha khang /
bde thabs lha khang sogs gsar btsugs dang /
gnas chung dgon pa gsar btab /
gzhan yang dbus gtsang kun tu dge dgon mang po gsar du bzhengs /
dga' ldan khri pa zhe brgyad kyi rnam thar dang dbus gtsang khams gsum du yod pa'i dge dgon ji yod kyi ming dang /
grwa grangs /
mchod gzhis sogs gsal bar 'khod pa'i <<dge ldan chos 'byung bai DUra ser po>> gsar du brtsams /
rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro cog rgyal rtse them spangs ma dpe gzhir byas nas rin po che sna tshogs dang /
gser chos /
skya chos bcas tshar brgya phrag lhag bzhengs te 'phyongs rgyas phying ba stag rtse dang /
'ol dga' stag rtse sogs rgya khyab rdzong gzhis rnams la bzhugs su bcug khyad par 'phyongs rgyas phying ba stag rtser /
bu ston rin po che'i bstan 'gyur dkar chag rtsa gzhir bzung de'i thog chos tshan nyis brgya bcu dgu gsar du bsnan te /
bstan 'gyur pod nyis brgya bco lnga yod pa gsar du  bzhengs /
<<dkar chag byin rlabs nyer 'bab>> ces pa brtsams /
tA la'i lnga pa yan gyi gsung 'bum rnams legs bsgrigs thog dkar chag kyang gsar du mdzad /
sde srid sangs rgyas rgya mtsho ni chos dang 'jig rten gang la'ang mkhyen pa mkha' ltar yangs shing /
spobs pa ri bo ltar mtho ba /
rang cag gangs can pa dag la lhag bsam bzang po nam yang nyams pa med pa zhig yin par ma tshad /
thun mong dang thun mong min pa'i rig gnas mtha' dag la mkhas shing /
khyad par gso ba rig pa dang rtsis kyi rig pa la mkhas pa'i yang rtser son /
rang re bod kyi gso ba rig pa dang rtsis rig 'phel rgyas 'gro ba'i lo rgyus thog dus rabs gsar pa zhig gi sgo legs par phye /
khong dgung grangs nyer bzhir phebs pa me 'brug lor lnga pa chen po'i zhal bkod ltar lcags po ri la !!rig byed 'gro phan gling'' zhes pa'i sman rtsis slob grwa gsar du btsugs /
slob ma bzhi bcu lhag bsdus /
slob grwa'i sgrig yig kyang gsal bar bkod /
lo ltar bod zla bdun pa'i nang lha sa'i nye skor dogs bde dang /
nyang bran /
brag yer pa sogs kyi ri khul du slob ma 'khrid de sman 'thu ru 'gro ba'i srol btsugs /
sde srid rang nyid ngo phebs kyis sngo sman re re bzhin gyi ro bro ba dbyibs kha dog bcas slob mar ngo sbyor byed pa'i slob srol spel /
dgung lo so brgyad la phebs pa lcags rta lor grwa thang rgyud bzhi la snon 'phri dag bcos thog rgyud bzhi gzhan dang go bsdur gyis shing par gsar du brkos /
rgyud bzhi'i dgongs 'grel <<bai DUra sngon po>> dang /
man ngag rgyud kyi kha skong le'u chig brgya so gsum yod pa'i <<lhan thabs>> bod kyi gso rig skor gyi lo rgyus <<khog 'bub drang srong dgyes pa'i dga' ston>> bcas snga phyir gsar du brtsams /
sman gzhung le'u chig brgya nga drug gi nang don cha tshang go rim dang ldan par bris pa'i sman dpe'i thang ga bdun cu don dgu gsar du bzhengs /
gna' rabs su bod kyi gso ba rig pa 'di la phal pa'i spyod yul las 'das pa'i lha sgrung lta bu'i seng ras kyis g.yogs pa bsal te /
don dngos dang sbrel nas slob khrid byed pa'i srol bzang po spel /
de nas bzung khams sde dge dpal spungs dang /
mdo smad bla brang bkra shis 'khyil sogs dbus gtsang khams gsum du bod kyi gso ba rig pa'i gzhung lugs dang /
sman pa mkhas pa dbyar mtsho rgyas pa ltar 'phel rgyas su phyin /
rtsis rig pa'i skor la /
bod sngar yod kyi rtsis gzhung ma lus gcig tu bsdus te zhib bsdur dang mtha' dpyad yang yang mdzad de /
rtsis gzhung <<bai DUra dkar po>> dang <<bai DUra g.ya' sel>> <<dka' gnad sgo lcags dbye ba'i lde mig>> sogs yid rton tshad mar gzung chog pa'i legs bshad mang po brtsams /
gzhan yang snyan ngag sgra /
bzo /
zlos gar sogs tha snyad rig pa'i bstan bcos kyang snyan zhing 'jebs pa 'ga' brtsams te rang cag phyi rabs pa dag la nam yang brjed du med pa'i mdzad rjes bzhag yod /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i lcags sbrul lo la bstan 'dzin dbang rgyal 'das par brten sde srid mchog nas lha bzang khang dbus su bos te bod sdod sog rgyal gyi go sar bzhag pa red /
lha bzang gis sog rgyal gyi go ming 'dzin nas bzung sde srid sangs rgyas rgya mtshor rgol ba'i 'khrug rtsod kho na bslangs /
khos sde srid 'dis rnying ma gtso bor byas pa las dge ldan par dga' zhen  mi 'dug ces dang /
bstan 'dzin dbang rgyal dug gis bsad pa red zer ba sogs 'chal gtam sna tshogs la brten nas se 'bras dge gsum dang sde srid bar dbyen dkrug byas /
tha na lha bzang gis lkog gsod pa 'ga' zhig btang nas sde srid kyi drung 'khor dmar bsad btang ba sogs gdug rtsub kyi bya ngan mang po brtsams te dbus lha ldan gyi gnas tshul ha cang mi bde bar gyur /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i shing bya lo'i smon lam chen mo'i skabs su bde 'jags dang /
lha bzang mi ngan 'di dbus nas bskrad pa'i ched du /
ta' la'i tshangs dbyangs rgya mtshos gtso bor mdzad pa'i bla ma las sne /
mchod yon /
sbyin bdag che dgu 'dzom pa'i dbus su /
sde srid nas srid kyi 'gan dbang dgongs zhu mdzad /
khong gi rigs sras ngag dbang rin chen sde srid du bskos /
lha bzang khang sog rgyal gyi go gnas rang 'jags thog mtsho sngon du btegs nas bsdad rgyur thag bcad /
de nas lha bzang khang la sde srid bkrongs nas bod kyi rgyal por 'dug rgyu'i ham sems ma 'grub pa'i thog mu mthud nas dbus lha ldan du btsan sdod bya rgyu'i go skabs kyang shor bar brten /
khong khro gting nas bslangs te mtsho khar bteg khul gyi g.yo 'phrul la brten nas /
byang nag chur slebs ma thag de gar sog dmag yod tshad ngan bsdu byas /
lha bzang gi skye sman tshe ring bkra shis kyis sne 'khrid pa'i sog dmag 'bor chen stod lung snang rtser 'dzul /
skabs der sde srid sangs rgyas rgya mtshos dbus lha ldan gyi gtsug lag khang dang se 'bras sogs kyi rten dang brten par bcas pa la bar chad mi 'byung ba dang /
lha sar 'khrug zing mi yong ba'i ched du /
sde srid sku 'khor nyung zad bcas gong dkar rdzong du phebs /
sog dmag gis gnas tshul de thos 'phral dmag mang po gong dkar du btang /
bod dmag gis dpa' ngar chen pos 'thab kyang mang sne nyung bas non ma thub par bod dmag bzhi brgya tsam rang srog blos btang byas kyang phan pa ma byung bar /
rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i shing bya lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu bdun nyin sog po btsan 'dzul dmag gi 'dre lag 'og sde srid rin po che'i sku'i me tog 'thor bar byas so / /
khong gi gsung ni ha cang mang po zhugs yod kyang dkar chag gsal po zhig de snga mi 'dug cing /
klong rdol gsung <<bka' gdams pa dang dge lugs pa'i bla ma rags rim gyi gsung 'bum mtshan tho>> nang du par du 'khod pa chos tshan so gsum la shog ldeb drug stong brgyad brgya brgyad cu yod pa dang /
par la ma 'khod pa pod drug yod par gsungs /
nged dpe mdzod khang du bai sngon /
bai dkar /
bai ser /
du kU la'i gos bzang sogs pod che chung bcu lhag tsam bzhugs shing du kU la pod gsum po ni lnga pa'i gsung 'bum du'ang nga pa dang /
ca pa /
cha pa byas te bkod 'dug go /

paN chen er te ni sku phreng rim byon gyi gsung 'bum / /
... @# / /
mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang gi gsung 'bum / /
... par ma /
... ka mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum ka pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa'i rnam thar mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsan yig bzhugs so / /
... mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung thor bu'i gras rnams phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa bzhugs so / /
... zab mo stong pa nyid kyi de kho na nyid rab tu gsal bar byed pa'i bstan bcos skal bzang mig 'byed ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi mthar thug pa'i lta ba thal 'gyur du 'grel tshul gnad don gsal ba'i zla zer bzhugs so / /
... 'grel pa don gsal gyi rnam bshad rtogs dka'i snang ba zhes bya ba mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen  pas mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... kha mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum kha pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... phyin ci log gi gtam gyi sbyor ba la zhugs pa'i smra ba ngan pa rnam par 'thag pa'i bstan bcos gnam lcags 'khor lo zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel chen dri ma med pa'i 'od kyi rgya cher bshad pa de kho na nyid snang bar byed pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... ga mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... 'grel chen dri med 'od kyi nang le'i 'grel bshad bzhugs so / /
... 'grel chen dri med 'od kyi dbang gi le'u'i 'grel bshad kyi stod cha bzhugs so / /
... TIk chen dbang le'i smad cha zhang zhung pa chos dbang grags pas mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... dus 'khor TIk chen las sgrub thabs le'i zhang zhung pa chos dbang grags pas mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
...  par ma /
... nga mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum nga pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... dus 'khor TIk chen las ye shes le'u'i TIk+ka zhang zhung pa chos dbang grags pas mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... dus 'khor TIk+ka chen las dbang le'i smad cha rje blo gros chos skyong gis mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... dus 'khor TIk+ka chen las sgrub thabs le'u'i 'grel bshad blo gros chos skyong gis mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... ca mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum ca pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... dus 'khor TIk chen las ye shes le'u'i 'grel bshad blo gros chos skyong gis mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel chen dri med 'od kyi dka' gnas kyi zin bris /
rgyal ba tsong kha pa'i gsung bzhin mkhas grub rin po ches brjed byang du mdzad pa shin tu rnyed dka' ba bzhugs so / /
...  dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dgongs pa rab gsal bzhugs so / /
... c  par ma /
... cha mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum cha pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... dus kyi 'khor lo'i sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i sgrub thabs padma dkar po'i zhal lung bzhugs / /
... bcom ldan 'das dus kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs la mchod pa'i cho ga kun tu bzang po'i mchod sprin bzhugs so / /
... dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i thig rtsa bzhugs so / /
... dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i nye bar mkho ba'i zur 'debs bzhugs / /
... dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil chog gi ngag 'don go sla bar brjod pa bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i mngon rtogs kyi lhan thabs bzhugs so / /
... dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam dpal rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyi lhan thabs mkhas grub chen pos mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... bstan pa'i mnga' bdag mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i zhal las byung ba'i rgyud kyi zin bris bzhugs so / /
... sngags dang pha rol tu phyin pa'i sa lam gyi bgrod tshul gsal sgron dang sbyar ba bzhugs so / /
... 'grel chen dri ma med pa'i 'od bya ba'i nang gi le'u'i dka' gnas rnams kyi zin bris rags tsam zhig bzhugs so / /
...  bcom ldan 'das dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lU i pa'i lugs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bde chen rol mtsho zhes bya ba mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang pos mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... bde mchog dril bu lus dkyil gyi dbang du byas pa'i bskyed rim gyi dka' gnas 'ga' zhig bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i dus 'khor gyi sgrub thabs padma dkar po'i zhal lung la log rtog sel tshul 'di dpe shin tu dkon pas gsung 'bum 'dir bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... ja mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum ja pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... rgyud thams cad kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bskyed rim dngos grub rgya mtsho zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rim lnga'i gsal byed mkhas grub rjes snga rting zin bris su bstsal ba rnams phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa bzhugs so / /
... dpal brtag pa gnyis pa'i rnam par bshad pa rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyi gsang ba'i mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
...  par ma /
... nya mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum nya pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... bcom ldan 'das dpal kyai rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bde ba chen po'i 'jug ngogs zhes  bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal kyai rdo rje'i sgrub thabs 'khrul spong zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... dpal kyai rdo rje'i mchod 'phreng rdo rje sems dpa'i bsgom bzlas dang bcas pa bzhugs so / /
... kyai rdo rje'i zur 'debs kyi cho ga bzhugs so / /
... sdom pa gsum gyi rnam par bzhag pa mdor bsdus te gtan la dbab pa'i rab tu byed pa thub bstan rin po che'i byi dor zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rgyud sde spyi'i rnam par bzhag pa rgyas par bshad pa mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang pos mdzad pa bzhugs so / /
... dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i bskyed rim gyi rnam gzhag gsal ba'i gtsug rgyan bzhugs so / /
... par ma /
... ta mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa dge legs dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum ta pa'i dkar chag bzhugs so / /
... stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od kyi dka' ba'i gnas rnam par 'byed pa brjed byang gi yi ge mkhas grub chos rjes rje la gsan dus mdzad pa bzhugs so / /

mi stong phrag brgal bar rab byung gi sdom pa bstsal /

de nas rim bzhin bdag nyid chen pos mkhan po dang /

bsnyen cing bkur ba sogs re re bzhin brjod kyi mi langs pa'i mkhas btsun bzang gsum ldan pa'i go 'phang du mnga' rnyed /

... 'phags pa dkon mchog brtsegs pa'i mdo las 'dul ba rnam par gtan la dbab pa nye bar 'khor gyis zhus pa zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa rgyal sras spyod pa'i ngang tshul gsal ba'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rje btsun 'phags ma sgrol ma'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i 'grel pa phyi nang 'jigs brgyad kyis gtses pa'i ngal gso'i gling zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

... rnam par rgyal ma la brten nas rang gzhan gyi tshe sgrub bya tshul dang rje btsun sgrol dkar gyi sgo nas tshe sgrub bya tshul 'chi med bdud rtsi'i dpal ster zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

gtsang nyang smad kyi sa'i cha sngon pa tshab tshul khrims rgyal mtshan dang sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms gnyis kyi mtshan zur bsdus te yul gyi ming btags pas pa nam zhes grags par yab dpal ldan don grub dang /
yum 'chi med rgyal mo gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu gsum pa'i chu stag lor sku bltams /
tA la'i bla ma 'jam dpal rgya mtsho dang la mo chos skyong gnyis kyis paN chen sku gong ma'i yang srid yin par nges pa rnyed nas ngos 'dzin mdzad /
chu yos lor 'khrungs yul nas dga' ldan legs bshad chos gling du gdan zhu bskyangs /

sa sprel lor /
stod khul sa mtshams su gor+Sha bas dus gzir bslangs stabs re zhig nyen yol du dbus nas gdan zhu 'byor ba bzhin lha ldan du chibs bsgyur bskyangs /
de'i phyi lor rgyal ba rin po cher brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs 'bul ba'i maN+Dala ljags bshad paN chen rin po ches gnang /
de skabs dgung lo bdun las son med pas sku na phra stabs gra sgrig po zhig e yong snyam tshang mar blo g.yeng byung yod na'ang /
de las ldog ste gsung dpangs mtho la gsal dag snyan gsum gyi sgo nas zhum pa med par gnang /
der 'dus ser skya rnams shin tu  ngo mtshar zhing dad gus tshad med skyes /
rgyal ba rin po ches mkhan po dang yongs 'dzin paN+Dita chen pos las slob /
dga' ldan khri pa blo bzang smon lam gyis dus go ba mdzad pa'i drung nas dge tshul gyi bslab sdom bzhes /
lcags phag lor gor dmag stod shel dkar khul du btegs par brten am ban nas rgyal ba yab sras mgar thar phyogs su phebs dgos tshul zhus par skabs der se 'bras dge gsum gyi bla spyi nas nged rang tshos bsrung bar bya chog pas rgyal dbang yab sras gnyis po phyogs gzhan du phebs na mi 'thus pa'i gnas tshul nan zhu byas /
am ban gnyis kyis kyang dgongs mthun byas te mgar thar phyogs su ma phebs par lha ldan rang du bzhugs /
gong ma'i nang blon chen po hu si krung thang phebs nas rgyal ba yab sras mjal 'dzoms thog gong mar sku'i mtshams zhu dang hu si krung thang la bkur bzos sogs gang che mdzad /
tA la'i yongs 'dzin paN+Di ta ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi mdun nas lam rim bde lam gyi zab 'khrid sogs mdo sngags kyi dbang lung du ma gsan nas thugs su chud pa ma zad /
rje nyid kyi yongs 'dzin 'phar ma sngags chen blo bzang bstan 'dzin gyi drung nas dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i 'khrid lung zab bshad kyis brgyan pa sogs dbang lung mang po gsan /
me sbrul lo nas bsdus gzhung rigs pa'i rgya mtshos mtshon gzhung lugs chen po rnams la gsan sbyong mdzad /
ring por ma thogs par gzhung lugs rnam gzhag gi tshig don thugs su chud de tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi mtha' gcod spyi don dang bcas pa la shin tu mkhas par 'gyur /
tshig tsam dang 'ol spyi tsam gyis tshim pa ma yin par theg pa gsum gyi lam gyi gnas thams cad rigs pa'i lam nas rnyed thub par thugs btson shin tu che khar nyin rer shog bu mda' tshad ma bcu gsum bcu bzhi tsam re thugs 'dzin mdzad pa sogs mkhyen rab 'gran zla bral ba'i grags pa thob /
lcags bya lo rgyal ba 'jam dpal rgya mtshos mkhan po dang /
yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan 'dzin gyis las slob /
byang rtse chos rje mthu stobs rgya mtshos gsang ston /

rgyal ba rin po che'i sku mdun nas byang chub lam rim gyi dmar khrid sogs kyi ljags lung gsan /
chu khyi lor rje tsong kha pa yab sras dang rje blo bzang chos rgyan blo bzang ye shes /
skal bzang rgya mtsho bcas kyi gsung 'bum cha tshang dang /
rje blo bzang dpal ldan ye shes kyi gsung 'bum pod bzhi gser chos su yod pa'i 'phros dang bcas pa gser chos su bzhengs par mdzad /
dz+hai k+Shima las grub pa'i gsang bde 'jigs gsum gyi sku brnyan dang /

shing byi lor /
rgyal ba 'jam dpal rgya mtsho zhi bar gshegs pas dgongs rdzogs mchod sprin rgya che bsgrubs pa dang sbrags yang srid myur byon gsol 'debs shig kyang brtsams par mdzad /
sa 'brug lor gung thang du chibs bsgyur thog rgyal ba rin po che'i yang srid sprul sku'i gtsug phud bzhes /
mtshan blo bzang bstan pa'i 'byung gnas ngag dbang lung rtogs rgya mtsho zhes gsol /
de nas ra sgreng dang /
ri bo dga' ldan sogs la gnas gzigs dang 'brel dge 'dun la bsnyen  bkur mang 'gyed dang /
skye bo ser skya du mar chos sbyin gyis tshim par mdzad /
chu bya lor jo bo shAkya mu ne'i spyan sngar rje nyid nas mkhan po dang dga' ldan khri chen yongs 'dzin ngag dbang snyan grags nas las slob /
shar pa chos rje byang chub chos 'phel nas dus go ba sogs mdzad nas rgyal ba lung rtogs rgya mtshor rab byung dang /
dge tshul gyi sdom pa phul /
de nas dus mi ring bar shing phag lor rgyal ba rin po che sku gshegs pas dgongs rdzogs mchod sprin bsgrubs /
chu rta lor gong ma'i bka' bzhin dbus ljongs lha ldan du chibs bsgyur thog rgyal ba sku gong ma lung rtogs rgya mtsho'i yang srid kyi dgos gnas yod pa gsum gser bum nang mtshan byang blugs te dkrug 'don mdzad /
gser bum nas thon pa li thang sgron 'dogs kyi khye'u de bla lha'i lung brtag sogs gang sa nas nges rnyed rtse mthun byung ste ngos 'dzin bskyangs /
dbu skra gtsug phud bzhes te dge bsnyen dang /
dge tshul gyi bslab sdom rim pa bzhin phul /
mtshan ngag dbang blo bzang 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin tshul khrims rgya mtsho zhes gsol /
rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i shing bya lor gzhis ka rtser bkra shis kun skyob gling gi gtsug lag khang rten dang brten pa bcas gsar bzhengs /
gong mas man rgya bod sogs bcas yi ge bzhi gshibs kyi kun skyob gling zhes pa'i mtshan dang /
phA bya'i grong nyan zhes yig 'bru bzhi'i pan bod skad du bsgyur na chos sbyin gzi 'bar zhes pa'i gzengs bstod bstsal /
shing rta lor rje nyid nas mkhan po dang srid skyong sa ma Ti pak+Shisa las slob /
dga' ldan khri zur byang chub chos 'phel gyis gsang ston /

chu 'brug lor bkas bkod mdzad pa bzhin rim gyis pho brang gsar 'debs kyi dbu tshugs /
dge 'dun gyi kun dga' ra ba sogs rtse shod dang /

shing 'brug lor tshe smon gling no min han nas srid skyong mdzad skabs dza sag sogs nas las don 'thus tshang byung min la brten bka' nyes phog pa'i tshab paN chen rin po ches srid skyong gi mdzad 'khur bzhes /

rigs rus phun sum tshogs shing /
nor longs spyod ha cang mi phyug pa bar ma'i khyim tshang dwags brum dga' shar zhes par yum bstan chung mtsho mo'i sras su rab byung bco lnga'i chu lug lor sku bltams /
sa byi lor yang srid kyi dogs gnas dwags brum dga' shar dang /
la mo /
thob rgyal bcas su 'khrungs pa'i chung srid gsum gser bum dkrug 'don gyi brtag dpyad gnang rgyu'i ched /
rtse pho brang sa gsum rnam rgyal du rgyal ba mchod yon dang /
bod bzhugs am ban /
bkras lhun bla brang gi mi sna /
bum sgrub chog grwa ba sogs ser skya du ma gdan 'dzoms sar chung srid gsum gyi mtshan byang ba so'i byang bur bkod de gser bum nang blugs te lan gsum dkrugs  par dwags brum dga' shar du 'khrungs pa'i chung sring rin po che'i mtshan byang 'phar te thon par ma zad /
bla lha khag gi lung brtag sogs gang nas rtse mthun byung bar brten /
paN chen sku gong ma bstan pa'i dbang phyug gi yang srid du ngos 'dzin thog rgyal dbang thub bstan rgya mtshos mthon mthing dbu skra'i gtsug phud bzhes /
mtshan blo bzang thub bstan chos kyi nyi ma dge legs rnam rgyal zhes gsol bar gnang /
lha ldan gtsug lag khang yas mas la gnas gzigs kyi gnang sgo legs par grub ste /
bkra shis lhun por chibs bsgyur dang 'brel pho brang rgyal mtshan mthon po'i khri la mnga' gsol nas mdzad sgo gzab cing rgyas pa mdzad /
sku na phra ba'i dus nas dam pa'i rang rtags kyis mdzes pas skya bo tha mal pa las khyad du 'phags /
mdo sngags kyi mkhas btsun dam pa blo bzang bstan 'dzin dbang rgyal yongs 'dzin du bsten te /
dbang lung rjes gnang sogs kyi chos bka' mang po gsan /
phyag bris 'bri klog gis mtshon rig gnas khag la gsan sbyong mdzad /
chu stag lor bkra shis lhun po nas dbus ljongs lha ldan du chibs bsgyur gnang ste rgyal ba thub bstan rgya mtshos mkhan slob sbrags ma dang /
dga' ldan khri gdan zur /
shar byang chos rje sogs 'dul ba 'dzin pa grangs tshang ba'i dbus su dge bsnyen dang /
bar ma rab byung sngon du 'gro bas tshigs snga ma dge tshul dang /
bslab gzhi yongs su rdzogs pa'i dge slong gi sdom pa bcas rim bzhin bzhes /
bsrung bya'i bcad mtshams gtsang mar mdzad pas btsun pa'i yon tan mchog tu gyur /
de nas mtshan nyid kyi gzhung lugs bka' pod lnga la go rim ldan pa'i thugs gnyer gnang /
tshig don kun la thos bsam gyis sgro dogs legs par bcad de mkhas pa'i rtser son /

dkyil khang legs bshad gling /
shar rtse bsam gtan gling bcas grwa tshang gsum la 'jam dbyangs dmar ser /
'jam dbyangs dkar po /
'jam dbyangs smra seng bcas kyi snang brnyan zhal thang bzang gos kyi gsham lag can re thugs dam gyi rten du sbyor 'bul thog mchod sprin dang /
dge 'dun 'dus tshogs su bsnyen bkur mang 'gyed bcas gzab rgyas spros /
theg chen bstan bcos mngon rtogs rgyan gyi 'grel pa bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal po dang /
dkyil khang legs bshad gling par phar phyin spyi don dang /
tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi dgongs don gsal bar byed pa'i mtha' dpyod lung rigs gter mdzod ces pa par bskrun mdzad /
shing yos lor bkra shis lhun por gser zangs las bsgrubs pa'i rje btsun byams pa mgon po'i sku brnyan mtho tshad khru brgya tsam yod pa zhig bzhengs /
de ni 'dzam gling du gser zangs kyi sku brnyan che shos shig yin /
sa lug lor byams sku'i spyan sngar gser sbyangs las bskrun pa'i snang gsal gyi yol go rin chen phra tshoms kyis mchog tu spud pa zhig 'bul gnang mdzad /
chu phag lor bkra shis lhun po nas sog yul brgyud pe cing sogs su chibs bsgyur gnang /

pe cing yin da'i pho brang du bzhugs skabs sum cu pa'i snying po legs bshad  ljon dbang gi 'grel pa zhig bka' rtsom mdzad /

go ming tang srid gzhung gis mtshan 'phar g.yang Ti'i tham ga zhig 'bul bzhes kyi rten 'brel bskyangs /

... bde bar gshegs pa'i rten sgrub tshul dang /
de'i phan yon bstan pa rin po che spungs pa zhes bya ba dang /
legs bshad gser gyi phreng ba bcas bzhugs so / /
... rnying ma dang bon gyi rnam gzhag bzhugs so / /
... sngags kyi bslab bya /
smon sems kyi bslab bya /
skyabs 'gro'i bslab bya rnams bzhugs so / /
... gshin po dman mchog la phan gdags tshul bzhugs so / /
... 'jig rten bya ba'i rnam par bshad pa mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog ces bya ba bzhugs so / /
... rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus nyung bsdus /
... spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan ni /
rab byung bdun pa'i chu rta spyi lo nas rab byung brgyad pa'i chu 'brug spyi lo bar dgung lo bdun cu don gcig bzhugs /
'khrungs yul lha sa'i shar phyogs rgya ma  rin chen sgang dgon pa'i nye 'dabs su yab dgyer rigs chos skyabs dang /
yum jo mo bla 'bum gnyis la spyan snga sku mched gnyis byung ba'i chung ba yin /
dgung lo bdun lon skabs khu bo rin po che kun dga' blo gros kyi drung du rab byung mdzad /
mtshan la blo gros rgyal mtshan zhes btags /
rje tsong kha pa dang /
rgyal tshab rje /
mkhas grub rje /
'dul 'dzin grags pa rgyal mtshan /
skyor mo lung mkhan chen chos rgyal dpal bzang /
rtogs ldan 'jam dpal rgya mtsho sogs bla ma mang du bsten nas dge lugs dang bka' brgyud kyi chos mang po gsan /
rgya ma rin chen dgon pa'i gdan sa zla ba bco brgyad tsam mdzad pa las /
sku tshe gcig ring sgrub pa nyams bzhes gtso bor gnang ste /
skabs re slob ma rnams la mdo sngags kyi chos gsungs /
gsung rtsom gyi skor la blo sbyong /
lam rim /
lta khrid /
'dul ba'i bslab bya /
gsang sngags kyi bskyed rdzogs /
bla ma'i rnam thar /
zhal gdams dang 'phrin yig la sogs pa'i gsung rtsom shog grangs bzhi brgya lhag tsam byas pa'i pod chen gsum nged dpe mdzod khang du yod / /
...  rtsom sgrig byed mkhan gyi ming tho /
rtsom sgrig pa gtso bo /
sun lbun jing /
rtsom sgrig pa gzhon pa /
mi nyag mgon po /
thang khri an /
rtsom sgrig gi bya bar gzhug mkhan /
gsham du rus ming gi rgya yig smyug 'gros mang nyung ltar bsgrigs pa mi nyag mgon po /
sun lbun jing /
thang khri an /
kra'o ping ru /
kho h+pheng ming /
thang khra'o phan /
rtsom sgrig dang zhu dag gi bya ba 'ga' la gzhug mkhan /
dung dkar blo bzang 'phrin las /
blo bzang chos 'byor /
don dbang bsod nams stobs rgyal /
ku'o yon shing /
dpe deb 'di rtsom sgrig byed pa'i bya rim nang /
krung dbyang mi rigs slob grwa chen mo dang /
bod rang skyong ljongs spyi tshogs tshan rig khang /
pe cin dpe mdzod khang /
krung go nang pa'i chos tshogs bcas kyis rogs ram chen po gnang yod pa dang /
gsung 'bum gyi chos tshan re re'i kha byang rgya yig tu sgyur ba phal cher sku zhabs ku'o ho chin nas sngar bsgyur zin pa'i ma yig la gzhir bzung ste dag bcos legs bsgrigs byas pa yin pas /
'dir nga tshos snying thag pa nas thugs rje che zhu rgyu yin /
...  dpe sgrig 'gan 'khur ba /
las dang len /
... shes bya'i gter mdzod /
mi rigs dpe mdzod khang gi dpe tho las gsung 'bum skor gyi dkar chag bar cha mi rigs dpe skrun khang gis bskrun zhing 'grems spel byas pa /
lo'i zla par par gzhi po bsgrigs pa /
lo'i zla par pe cin la par thengs po brgyab pa /
deb rer sgor .  ...
